1b1(rgyug): rgya gar skad du
2b1(rgyud): shrI gu h+ya sa mA dza
2b2(rgyud): nA ma bod skad du//
3a1(rgyud): dpal gsang ba 'dus pa zhes bya ba/ dpal rdo rje sems
3a2(rgyud): dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na bcom
3a3(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyi
3a4(rgyud): snying po rdo rje btsun mo'i pA ga la bzhugs so// brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang
3b1(rgyud): brjod kyis mi lung ba'i/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi ri rab kyi rdul phra rab snyed kyi/ byang chub sems dpa'
3b2(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dam tshig rdo rje dang
3b3(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sku rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
3b4(rgyud): po gsung rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thugs rdo rje dang / byang chub sems
3b5(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po ting nge 'dzin rdo rje dang // byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgyal
4a1(rgyud): ba rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa'
4a2(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po chu rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'i chen po mi rdo rje dang / byang
4a3(rgyud): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rlung rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
4a4(rgyud): po nam mkha' rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzugs rdo rje dang / byang chub
4a5(rgyud): sems dpa' sems dpa'i chen po sgra rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dri rdo rje dang // 
4a6(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ro rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
4b1(rgyud): reg bya rdo rje dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid rdo rje dang / de dag la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa'
4b2(rgyud): sems dpa' chen po brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul phra rab snyed rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs
4b3(rgyud): pa nam mkha'i dbyings dang mnyam pa la 'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje mi skyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad
4b4(rgyud): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rin chen dpal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje 'od dpag tu med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje
4b5(rgyud): gdon mi za ba dang / de dag la sogs pa nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs po rnams dang tha bas gcig tu
4b6(rgyud): bzhugs pa ni/ 'di lta ste/ dper na/ til gyi glang bu bzhin du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ nam mkha'i dbyings
4b7(rgyud): thams cad shin tu gang bar snang bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad chen po// de bzhin
5a1(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags chen po'i tshul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bkod pa de dag thams cad nyid kyi sku la
5a2(rgyud): zhugs par mdzad do// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad kyis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po// yongs su mnyes par
5a3(rgyud): bya ba'i phyir/ nyid kyi sku bud med kyi gzugs su mngon par ma sprul nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad chen po'i sku las mngon par byung bar gyur to// de la la la ni sangs rgyas spyan
5a4(rgyud): lci bu/ la lA ni mA ma ki lte bu/ la la gos dkor mo lta bu/ la la dam tshig sgrol ma lta bu/ la la gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid lta bu/ la la sgra'i ngo bo lta bu/ la la dri'i ngo bo lta bu/ la la
5a5(rgyud): ni ro'i ngo bo lta bu/ lnga la rig gi ngo bo lta bur/ der yang dag par gnas par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ma skyed pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi skye dang / 
5a6(rgyud): gsung dang thugs kyi snying po rdo rje btsun mo'i bA ga la/ dam tshig chen po'i dkyil 'khor rdul med pa gru bzhir byin gyis brlabos pa ni/ gsal ba de yi ngo bo nyid// sna tshogs gzug
5a7(rgyud): kyis kun tu rgyas// sangs rgyas smi naM gyis kun du khyab// 'od zer 'phro ba mang po 'khrug/ gsal ba la sogs dkyil 'khor ldan// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// de nas
5a8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i bdag po// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor chen po'i dbus su gzhag par gyur to// 
5b1(rgyud): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi skyod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gdon mi za bar grub pa dang / 
5b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje'i thugs la zhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems
5b3(rgyud): rdo rje// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po snyoms
5b4(rgyud): par zhugs ma thag tu/ de nas nam mkha'a'i dbyings 'di thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i ngo bor gnas par gyur to// de nas nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad na gnas pa'i sem
5b5(rgyud): can ji snyed pa de dag thams cad rdo rje sems dpa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba thob par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
5b6(rgyud): gshegs pa byang chub kyi sems rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i dam tshig 'byung ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rig pa
5b7(rgyud): chen po'i skyes bu'i gzugs 'di/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis byin gyi brlabs so// byin gyis brlabs ma thag tu// bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi sems
5b8(rgyud): rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa de nyid zhal gsum pa lta bur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gzigs par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa mi skyod pa la sogs pa bcom ldan
6a1(rgyud): 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs kha nas byung ste/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ byang chub sems ni rab byung ba// de bzhin gshegs
6a2(rgyud): pa kun gyi gsang/ rab tu mi rtog gnas med pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das dri bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang gcig tu 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi
6a3(rgyud): sems rdo rje la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mchod pa rgyas pa spros pa'i de kho na nyid kyi dam tshig rin po'i sprin gyis/ yang dag par mchod nas/ phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to/ 
6a4(rgyud): 'dus pa gsong ba las byung ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kan gyi gsang // rdo rje snying po btus pa yi// de nyid bcom ldan bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
6a5(rgyud): byang chub kyi sems rdo rjes// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad legs so logs so// 'on kyang 'di
6a6(rgyud): ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyang / the tsom skye bar byed pa yin na/ byang chub sems dpa' gzhan rnams lta ci smos/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshan
6a7(rgyud): du gyur/ rmad du gyur te/ the tsom thams cad gcod por mdzod pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to// gang bcom ldan 'das 'di lta
6a8(rgyud): bu'i yon tan khyad par can du gyur pa yang // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba ston par mi spro ba de/ 
6b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la byin gyis brlab pa mdzad de/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam chag rdo rje'i dam tshig 'byung ba'i tshig gis/ de bzhin gshegs
6b2(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi bde ba dang / yid bde ba myong bar bgyi ba nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes dang / mngon par shes pa'i 'bras bu thob par bgyi ba'i bar gyi phyir/ yang
6b3(rgyud): dag par bstan du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi
6b4(rgyud): gsol ba btab pa de mkhyen nas/ ye shes kyi sgron ma rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ zhe sdang gi rigs kyi mchog gi snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsang dang
6b5(rgyud): thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // badz+ra d+h+r-ig/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ dasku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu/ mi skyed pa'i
6b6(rgyud): phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis/ nag po dkar po dmar po'i tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje'i sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje la
6b7(rgyud): bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'byung ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ti nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ gti mug gi rigs mchog gi
6b8(rgyud): snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lasu phyung ngo // dzi na dzeg/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
7a1(rgyud): thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu rnam par snang mdzad kyi phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis dkar po nag po dmar po'i tshul du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku
7a2(rgyud): dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i spyan sngar bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che 'byung ba'i rdo rje/ dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par
7a3(rgyud): zhugs te/ yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rigs mchog gi snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // kA rad na d+h+ri ga/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
7a4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu rin chen dpal gyi phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thibs kyis/ ser po nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi
7a5(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i lho phyogs su bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ 'dod chags chen po 'byung ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
7a6(rgyud): par zhugs nas/ rdo rje 'dod chags kyi rigs kyi mchog gi snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // A ro lig/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu bcom ldan 'das de
7a7(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rig pa'i skyes bu 'jig rten dbang phyug gi rig pa'i bdag po phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis/ dmar po nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ de
7a8(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i rgya ga tu bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdon mi za ba'i mchog dam tshig 'byung ba'i rdo rje
7b1(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ dam tshig 'gugs pa'i rigs mchog gi snying po'i snying po 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // pradz+nyA d+h+rig/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ 
7b2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu grub pa gdon mi za ba'i phyag rgya chen por sbyor ba'i thabs kyis ljang khu nag po dkar po'i tshul du/ da
7b3(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i byang phyogs su bzhugs so// zhe sdang gti mug 'dod chags dung // yid bzhin nor bu dam tshig ste// rigs lhur gtogs pa 'di rnams
7b4(rgyud): kyis// 'dod dang thar pa rab sgrub pa'o// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje 'dzin rjes su mnyes par byed pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par
7b5(rgyud): zhugs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin thams cad kyi btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dwe sha ra tI/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
7b6(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu 'di nyid bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par gyur te/ shar phyogs kyi grwar bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
7b7(rgyud): thams cad rjes su mnyes par byed pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje
7b8(rgyud): lhas phyung ngo // ma~M ha ra ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu 'di nyid/ bud med kyi gzugs
8a1(rgyud): 'dzin par gyur te// lha phyogs kyi grwar bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags 'dzin pa rjes su chags par byed pa'i rdo rje zhe
8a2(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs thams cad kyi 'dod chags 'dzin pa btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // ra ga ra ti
8a3(rgyud): do nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu 'dri nyid/ bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par gyur te// nub
8a4(rgyud): phyogs kyi grwar bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tha mas cad kyi sgra dang gsung dang thugs sla ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin
8a5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab 'chang ba'i btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // badz+ra ra ti/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de
8a6(rgyud): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ bud med kyi gzugs 'dzin par gyur te/ byang phyogs kyi grwar bzhugs so// de bzhin gshegs pa/ 
8a7(rgyud): thams cad kyi btsun mo'i mchog phun sum tshogs pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad rdo rje 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin
8a8(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // ya man ta bi kring / de nas 'di phyung ma
8b1(rgyud): thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad snyengs par byed pa'i tshul du/ shar phyogs
8b2(rgyud): kyi sgor bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mngon par byang chub bya/ rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa
8b3(rgyud): thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // pradz+nyA ta bkrid/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das
8b4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid rdo rje dam tshig bsnyengs par byed pa'i tshul du/ lho phyogs kyi sgor bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan
8b5(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos rin po che 'byung gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'dod chags 'chang ba'i
8b6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi sku dang / gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // pad ma ta bkrid/ de nas 'di phyung ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
8b7(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi tshul du/ nub phyogs kyi sgor bzhugs so// 
8b8(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
9a1(rgyud): cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i khro bo chen po 'di nyid kyi/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // 
9a2(rgyud): big+hA ta bkrid de nas 'di phyung ma thog tu/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhi ni gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi rig pa'i skyes bu de nyid/ de bzhin gshegs pa
9a3(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyi tshul du/ byang phyogs kyi sgor bzhugs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ sku dang dang / gsung dang / thugs mnyes pa byed pa
9a4(rgyud): dang / dkyil 'khor gyi dam tshig sems dpa' rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs
9a5(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
9a6(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi bdag po la/ bcom ldan 'dis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis mchod pa byas te/ phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces gsol to// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi mchog/ 
9a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // bla na med pa'i byang chub sems// bcom ldan snying po bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
9a8(rgyud): dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsol ba btab par mkhyen cing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sems kyi yongs su rtog pa yang thogs// 
9b1(rgyud): kyis mkhyen nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// khyed kyi sems lus lta bu dang // lus sems lta bu dang / sems tshig tu brjod pa lta bur bskyed
9b2(rgyud): cig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gis/ de bzhin gshugs pa thams cad kyi/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs nam mkha' lta bur sbyar nas/ chen
9b3(rgyud): / du brjod pa 'di/ ched du brjod do// e ma'o kun du bzang po yi// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje can// skye ba med pa'i tshul gyis su/ skye ba 'di ni rib tu bsgrags// de nas bcom
9b4(rgyud): ldan 'das/ de bzhin gshegs pa tha mams cad kyi/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhi ni gshegs pa thams cad kyi mngon par byang chub pa'i
9b5(rgyud): tshul rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dngos po med pa sgom pa med// sgom par bya ba dngos po min// de ltar dngos
9b6(rgyud): po dngos med pa/ sgom pa dmigs su med pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'dres de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs
9b7(rgyud): so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mngon par rtogs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi
9b8(rgyud): sems 'di gsungs so// dngos po thams cad dang bral ba// phung po khams dang skye mched dang // gzung dang 'dzin pa rnam spangs pa// chos bdag med pa mnyam nyid pa// rang
10a1(rgyud): // sems bzod nas ma skyes pa// stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin no// zhes bcom ldan 'das/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyis gsungs so// de nas
10a2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das/ de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje ma skyed pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ mi zad pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub
10a3(rgyud): kyi sems 'di gsungs so// dngos po 'di rnams ma skyes pas// chos dang chos nyid med pa ste// nam mkha' lta bur bdag med pa// byang chub tshul 'di brtan pa'o// 
10a4(rgyud): zhes bcom ldan 'das/ de bzhin gshegs pa mi skyod pas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das/ de bzhin gshegs pa rin chen dpal/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
10a5(rgyud): kyi bdag med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos rnams thams cad dngos med cing // chos kyi mtshan
10a6(rgyud): nyid rnam par spangs// bdag med chos las kun du byung // byang chub tshul 'di brtan pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa/ rin chen dpal gyis
10a7(rgyud): gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa 'od zer bya bar ba/ rdo rje sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs
10a8(rgyud): te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// ma skyes pa yi chos rnams la// ngo bo med de sgom pa'ang med// nam mkha'i tshul du sbyor ba yis// de ltar
10b1(rgyud): dngos po rab tu bsgrags// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa gdon mi za ba// 
10b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ byang chub kyi sems 'di gsungs so// chos rnams rang bzhin 'od gsal ba/ 
10b3(rgyud): gdod nas dag pa nam mkha' bzhin// byang chub med cing mngon rtogs med// byang chub tshul 'di brtan pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa gdon mi za bas
10b4(rgyud): gsungs so// de nas bems pa la sogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'o chen po rnams/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ka/ sku dang / gsang dang / thugs kyi gsang ba
10b5(rgyud): chos kyi de kho na nyid kyi yi ga thos nas/ ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur te/ ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma'o sangs rgyas e ma'i cho tos bshad pa ni ngo ma tshar che
10b6(rgyud): yang dag don ni dag pa'i don/ byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// bdag med pa yi chos las blang // sangs rgyas byang chub rdzogs mdzad bya mi rtog dmigs su med/ 
10b7(rgyud): byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// kun du bzang po thams cad don// byang chub sems ni rab bskor ba// byang chub spyod pa rdo rje che// byang chub sems la ngaga'aphrul lo// dag pa de bzhin gshogs
10b8(rgyud): po'i thugs// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas byang chub rab ston pa// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang
11a1(rgyud): pa 'dus pa las byang chub kyi sems kyi le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo / de bzhin gshegs
11a2(rgyud): pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'phro ba'i sprin bkod pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u 'di gsungs so// oM shu n+ya
11a3(rgyud): ta dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+ha wa ad ma ko hau/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor sgom pa ni// 'od zer sprin gyi tshogs chen po// sangs rgyas 'bar ba'i 'od dang mnyam/ 'od
11a4(rgyud): zer sna lngas kun du khyab// kun nas yongs su zlum po rau te// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis khya ba// mchod pa rnam pa lngas rgyan pa// mdor na de ltar bsgoms nas su// gzugs ni dbus su sgom par bya// rnam
11a5(rgyud): par snang mdzad phyag rgya che// sku gsung thugs kyis mtshan pa'o// sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje yis// phyag rgya'am yang na sgom par bya// tshogs gnyis dang ni ldan pa yis// mi skyod pa yi rgya mchog dang // dkon
11a6(rgyud): mchog dpal gyi rgya chen dang // tshe dpag med pa'i 'od byed dang // thigs med 'grub pa'i rgya chen rnams// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// in dra ni la'i kha dog
11a7(rgyud): 'dra// rab 'bar phyag na rdo rje bsnams// rnam par gtsigs la 'jigs 'jigs lha// shel dang zla ba'i 'od 'dra ba// thor btsugs con pan gyis rgyan pa// rab 'bar phyag na 'khor lo bskams// sa
11a8(rgyud): tshogs rgyan gyis mdzes par brgyan/ 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser 'od 'dra/ sangs rgyas sprin gyis kun tu 'khrigs// de yi phyag na rdo rje che/ rtse mo dgu par rnam par/ bsgom
11b1(rgyud): ma rgad ta yi 'od 'dra ba// rdo rje 'bar pas rnam par rgyan// kun du 'bar ba'i sprin gyis khyab// phyag na rin chen bsnams par sgom// pad ma ra ga'i mdog 'dra ba// gtso bo 'dod chags 'bar ba mnga'// rab 'bar phyag na pad ma
11b2(rgyud): bsnams// 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgom pa// 'od zer sna lnga'i 'od 'dra'i sku// gdon mi za ba rdo rje can+da// zhi ba phyag na ral gri bsnams// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
11b3(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsang dang thugs rdo rjed bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sku dang gsung dang thugs byin gyis rlob pa'i sngags 'digs
11b4(rgyud): so// oM d+harma d+ha du sAM b+ha wa ad ma ko haMHrin chen chen po kha dog lnga// nyungs dkar gyi ni bru tshod tsam// sna yi rtse mor nan tan du// rnal 'byor pa yis rtag par sgom// rin chen brtan par gyur nas spro// brtan par ma gyur yong mi
11b5(rgyud): smoHsangs rgyas 'bar ba 'dra ba'i 'od// mchog rab sprin rnams spro bar bya// 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen dang // pad ma ral gri mtshon tshwa 'dzin// byang chub sems dpa'i sprin chen rnams// spro ba'i bdag nyid can gyis spro/ 
11b6(rgyud): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rdo rje dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// pad ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dra bar ni/ bzlas pa sgom pas
11b7(rgyud): bsgom par bya/ rin chen dkyil 'khor 'dra bar ni// rin chen brtson pas bsgom par bya// sbyor ba'i dkyil 'khor las byung ba// nam mkha' 'dra bar dri bar bya// 'di dag sangs rgyas rab kyi mchog// sku gsung thugs ni sgoms
11b8(rgyud): pa yis// dkyil 'khor rdo rje las byung ba// thams cad mkhyen tshul 'thob pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'angs pa las rdo rje bkod pa zhi ba bI ting 'i dzi gyi'i bu steg sum pa'o// / 
12a1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang / thugs kyi bdag po la/ bstod pa'i rgyal
12a2(rgyud): po 'dis gsol ba btab po// de bzhin gshegs pa kun zhi ba// dri bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// chos kun bdag med pa yi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// mtshan rnams thams/ 
12a3(rgyud): cad yang dag rdzogs// mtshan min thams cad yang dag spangs// kun du bzang po swa yi mchog/ dkal 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// zhi ba'i chos ni mchog las byung // ya shes smod pa rnam spong bkun
12a4(rgyud): du bzang po gsung gi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// sems can kun gyi sems chen po// rang bzhin dag cing dri ma med// kun bzang thugs mchog kha lo bsgyur// dkyil 'khor dam pa
12a5(rgyud): bshad du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// 'jig rten gsum pa khams gsum pa// 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtso// 'jig rten gsum mchog ston pa pos// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas
12a6(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor rab 'dra ba// dkyil 'khor rab tu nyams dga' bshad// de nas thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ thugs kyi rdo rje rab 'dra ba/ sku dang gsung dang
12a7(rgyud): thugs rnams kyi// dkyil 'khor rab tu bshad par bya// lus ngag sems ni bsgoms pa yis// shes rab can gyis thig btab pas// thig skad sar pa legs bkal ba// tshad ma rab tu mdzes pa yis// thugs
12a8(rgyud): kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa ste// khru ni bcu gnyis tshad du bya// ngos bzhi dang ni grwa bzhir ldan// sgo bzhi par ni rab tu brtag/ de yi dbus su 'khor lo ni// rab tu zlum por bri bar bya// de nas las kyi cho ga ni// 
12b1(rgyud): mthong bas phyag rgya dgod par bya// de dbus rdo rje bri ba ni// in dra ni la'i kha dog 'dra// 'bar ba chen po rtse lnga pa// 'jigs pa dag kyang rab 'jigs byed// 'khor lo chen po shar phyogs su// rdo rje 'bar bas
12b2(rgyud): rnam par brgyan// rin chen chen po lho phyogs su// 'od zer mang po rab tu 'khrigs// padad+ma mo chen po nub phyogs su// pad ma ra khwa'i kha dog 'dra// ral gri chen po byang phyogs su// 'od zer mang pos rab tu 'khrig
12b3(rgyud): dbus na sprin dang 'dra ba'i 'od// spyan nau shar gyi gra ru bri// mA ma ka ni rigs byung ba'i// rdo rje de bzhin lho phyogs su// pad ma kha bye sdong por bcas// nub phyogs su ni bri bar bya// ud pal mdzes pa byang phyogs su// 
12b4(rgyud): 'thing kha sprin dang 'dra ba bri// tho ba 'bar ba 'od gsol pa// shar phyogs sgor ni bri bar bya// rdo rje' bar sogs 'od bzang ba// be con lho'i phyogs su bri// pad ma 'bar ba'i 'od byed pa// nub kyi phyogs su bri bar bya// 
12b5(rgyud): rdo rje 'khyil pa rdo rje can// byang gi phyogs su rdo rje bri// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa ste// yongs su gsal bar shes byas nas// lus dang ngag sems mchod pa yis nan tan du ni mchod par bya// bud med rab tu mdangs
12b6(rgyud): bzang ba// lo grangs bcu drug lon pa ni// dri dang me tog phreng brgyan te// yon tan ska rigs mA me ka re// shes rab can gyis byin brlabs la// de yi dbus su mnyes par bya// sangs rgyas zhi ba'i gnas spros pas// nam
12b7(rgyud): mkha'i dbyings ni rab tu brgyan// gshang gci khu ba khrag la sogs// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de ltar byas na sangs rgyas dang // byang chub sems dpa' grags chen mnyes// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi// 
12b8(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba// gsang ba 'dus pa las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ni// kun gyi sku dang
13a1(rgyud): / gsung thugs kyi/ rdo rje 'chang ba'i rgyal po ni// gnas kyi dbang phyug kun mchog gi// spyod pa kun mchog chos kyi don// spyod pa'i mtshan nyid bka' bsngal to// rnam par mi rtog don
13a2(rgyud): las byung // 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rigs// theg pa'i mchog ni bla med pa'i// dngos gru ba rab mchog sgrub par byed// rigs ngan smig ma mkhan la sogs// gsod don don gnyer sems pa rnams
13a3(rgyud): theg chen bla na med pa yi// theg mchog 'di la 'grub par 'gyur// sems can mtshams med la sogs pa'i// sdig pa chen po byed pa yang // rdo rje theg pa rgya mtsho che// theg pa mchog na 'di la 'grub// snying nas
13a4(rgyud): slob dpon smod pa dag/ bsgru bas kyang 'grub par mi 'gyur ro// srog gcod pa yi sems can gang // brdzun du smra ba dga' ba dang // gzhan gyi nor la chags pa dang // rtag tu 'dod pa spyod gang dang // gshad
13a5(rgyud): gci zas su za ba ste// de dag sgrub pa'i snod du 'gyur// ma dang sring mo bu mo la// 'dod pa pas ni mnyes byas na// theg chen mchog gi chos nyid kyi// dngos grub rgyo chen des thob po// sangs rgyas gtso bo'i yum
13a6(rgyud): dag la// rnam par ma rtog blo can gyis// mi nyes par byas kyang mi gos te// de ni sangs rgyas 'grub par 'gyur// de nas sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba la sogs pa// byang chub sems dpa' sems
13a7(rgyud): dpa' chen po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur// rmad du gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po ci'i slad du// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi nang du/ la 'di lta bu'i
13a8(rgyud): tshig ngan pa gsung zhes gsol to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi tshig gsan nas// 
13b1(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// rigs kyi bu rnams de skyed ma zer cig/ snying po ye shes can rnams kyi// sangs rgyas chos nyid dag pa 'di// snying po'i
13b2(rgyud): chos ni don las byung // byang chub spyod pa'i gnas 'di yin// de nas yang brjod kyis mi lang ba'i yang / brjod kyis mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ri rab la sogs pa'i rdul phra mo snyed kyi/ byang chub sems
13b3(rgyud): dpa' rnams 'jigs skrag nas rgyal bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis// byang chub sems dpa' de dag rgyal bar gyur pa gzigs nas// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
13b4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi spyi dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'di dag bslang bar gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
13b5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs/ rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa nam mkha' dang mnyam pa// gnyis su med pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// snyoms par
13b6(rgyud): zhugs ma thag tu/ bcom ldan 'das sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag po'i 'od kyis reg pa tsam gyis/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag rang rang gi snyan la gnas par
13b7(rgyud): gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur/ dgos pas khyab par gyur nas/ chos kyi dbyangs 'di skad ces gsungs so// e ma'o chos// e ma'o chos// e
13b8(rgyud): ma'o// chos kyi don 'byung ba// chos kyi don dag pa// bdag med pa/ rdo rje rgyal la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sku dang gsung thugs rabau tu dag/ nam mkha' dang ni mnyam nyid gnas// rnam par mi 'gyur snang
14a1(rgyud): ba med/ rdo rje'i sku la phyag 'tshal 'dud// thugs ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtso// dus gsum ngag gi lam du byung // nam mkha' chen po'i dbyings gyur pa// nam mkha'i
14a2(rgyud): lam la phyag 'tshal 'dud// nam mkha'i sku las yang dag 'byung // nam mkha'i lam la gnas pa po// nam mkha' thugs te chos kyi mchog/ spyod pa'i gnas la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs
14a3(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba// gsang ba 'dus pa las/ kun du spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste lnga pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje mi bskyod
14a4(rgyud): pa / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba/ rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ thugs byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// 
14a5(rgyud): oM saR+YA ta thA ga ta tsad twa badz+ra/ swa b+ha wa ad ma ko hi// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad/ rdul dang bral ba'i gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
14a6(rgyud): par zhugs te/ sku byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// / oM saR+YA ta thA ga ta kA yA/ badz+ra swa b+ha wa ad ma ko haM// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu
14a7(rgyud): med pa mnyam pa nyid mi gnyis pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ gsung byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM saR+Wa ta thA ga ta wag badz+ra swa b+ha b+ha ad ma ko haM/ rdo rje
14a8(rgyud): gsum po de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsar// gnas ni gnas kyis rnam par bsgom par bya// sngags kyi mtshan gyis shin du mtshan byas la// mchog rab 'di yis sgrub pa nyid du bya// de nas bcom
14b1(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog dpal ye shes sgron ma rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// / oM saR+Wa ta thA ga ta a nu rA ga na badz+ra swa b+ha wa ad
14b2(rgyud): mya ko haM// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa rdo rje gdon mi za ba/ rdo rje gdon mi za ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// 
14b3(rgyud): oM saR+Wa ta thA ga ta pu tsa badz+ra swa b+hA wa ad ma ko ho/ rtag tu 'dod pa'i yon tan lngas// sangs rgyas tshul bzhin mchod par bya// mchod pa rnam pa lnga rnams kyis// myur du sangs rgyasra nyid thob 'gyur/ 
14b4(rgyud): zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po rdo rje 'chang bas gsungs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
14b5(rgyud): thugs kyi bdag po rdo rje 'dzin gyis// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi gsang ba 'di gsungs so// sngags la dmigs pa'i lus dang ni// ngag dang yid kyis bskul nas su// yid ni dga' zhing
14b6(rgyud): mgo ba yis// dngos grub rab mchog bslub par bya// semase la dmigs pa bdag med pas// ngag dang lus kyang rnam par bsgom// nam mkha' bzhin du mnyam pa'i gnas// sbyor ba rnam gsum bslu ba pA/ 
14b7(rgyud): byata ts+tsho lus dang ngag dang sems dmigs ni// ngo bo nyid ni dmigs su med// sngags kyi las su sbyor ba la// byang chub med cing sgom pa med// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan nyid du// 'di ni mdor na rnam spyad
14b8(rgyud): nis// sngags kyis brtags pa'i ting nge 'dzin// byang chub sbyor ba bsgom par bya// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis mchod// sangs rgyas kun mchog kun mkhyen gyis/ 
15a1(rgyud): / sgom pa'i mchog ni bka' bstsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings ni dbus gnas par// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas gzugs ni rab bsgoms nas// phra mo'i
15a2(rgyud): slor ba kun du bsam// swa yi rtse mor yungs dkar bsam// 'gro dang mi 'gro yungs dkar la// ye shes gnas ni nyams dga' ba// gsang ba'i ye shes kyis brtags sgom// nam mkha'i dbyings
15a3(rgyud): kr-i dbus gnas par// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas sku yi gnas bsgoms te// de yi steng du gnas gzhag go// hUM nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas pa// gsal ba'i dkyil
15a4(rgyud): 'khor bsgom par bya// spyan gyi tshul du sbyor ba la// rdo rje pad mo rnam par sgom// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rin chen dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// dang po'i sbyor ba nan tan gyis
15a5(rgyud): de yi steng du yongs so sgom// nam mkha'i de byings kyi dbus gnas par// pad mo'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// gsung gi rdo rje tshul sbyor bar// 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgom pa// nam mkha'i da byi/ 
15a6(rgyud): kyi dbus gnas par// 'od kyi dAkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas tshul ni zhi ba spro// 'khor dang khyad par dag tu spro// ud pa la 'thing kha'i mdog 'dra ba// rtse mo lnga pa khyad par du// nas kyi
15a7(rgyud): 'a bru tsam nan tan gyis// sna yi rtse mor rnam par bsam// tsa na ka yi 'bru tsam la// mad ba ma brgyad pa gsar bcas// sna yi rtse mor 'di shis te// bsgoms pas byang chub gzhonu par 'gyur// 
15a8(rgyud): 'khor lo la sogs khyad par du// skom pa de ni brtag par bya// dngos grub thams cad yon tan gnas// nyams dga' byang chub gnas 'grub 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub gnas rnams ni// 
15b1(rgyud): de ru mdon na spro bar bya// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan pa yis// chos kyi tshig rnams rab tu brjod// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// de nyid don kun ston pa pos// spyod pa kun mchog legs dag pa// gsang ba'i
15b2(rgyud): dam tshig bka' bstsal to// gzugs dang sgra dang ror ldan par// shes rab can gyis zla drug sgom// gsang ba'i de nyid mchod chen gyis// legs par mchod nas bsgom par bya// dngos grub 'bras bu 'dod pa
15b3(rgyud): yis// zas su gshing gci zos na ni// sangs rgyas byang chub skyon med pa// yang dag bla myed 'grub par 'gyur// zlas su sha rnams za ba dang // sha chen dag ni rab brtags no// sku dang gsung dang thugs gas
15b4(rgyud): ba'i// dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// glang po'i sha dang rta yi sha// de bzhin dam pa khyi yi sha// zas kyi phyir ni bza' bar bya// zas gzhan dag ni ma zos na// byang chub sems dpa' blo can dang // 
15b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas rnams ni mnyes par 'gyur// 'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yis// myur du sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur// 'dod khams dbang phyug 'jig rten na// go 'phang las ni byed par 'gyur// gtso bo gzi
15b6(rgyud): can stobs dang ldan// mdang bzang mthong na yid du 'ong // mthong ba tsam gyis bskul ba yis// 'jig rten 'di dag pa dbang du 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba byang chub dam pa ste// 
15b7(rgyud): yang dag sngags kyi gsang ba 'di// lus ngag sems lus 'da' ba'o// / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las
15b8(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs byin gyis rlob pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag pos dam tshig chen po'i de kho
16a1(rgyud): na nyid sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i le'u 'di gsungs so// / 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la'ang // ji ltar 'dod par bsnyen na
16a2(rgyud): ni// 'di lta bu yi sbyor ba yiso// sangs rgyas myur du thob par 'gyur// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad ni// ji ltar 'dod pa bsten byas te// rang gi lha yi sbyor ba yis// bdag dang
16a3(rgyud): gzhan la mchod par bya// dka' thab sdom pa mi bzad pas// bsnyen kyang 'grub par mi 'gyur gyi// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la// bsnyen na myur du 'grab par 'gyur// slongs mo
16a4(rgyud): za zhing mi bzlas te// slong la'ang dga' bar mi bya'o// 'dod pa kun la longs spyod cing // sngags kyi yan lag ma nyams bzlas// lus dang ngag dang sems dang ni// bde bar gnas na byang
16a5(rgyud): chub thob// gzhan du dus min 'chi ba dang // dmyal bar nges par bsreg par 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // sngags kyi spyod pa mchog spyod rnams// chos mchog mi g.yo
16a6(rgyud): brnyis pa yang // 'dod pa thams cad bsten pas so// chags can ye shes 'dod pa yis// rtag tu 'dod yon lnga rnams bsten// byang chub sems dpa' mnyes par bya// byang chub sems
16a7(rgyud): nyi ma chags par bya// gzugs la rnam gsum shes byas nas// mchod par byed pas mchod par bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa// sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzod gzhi// snrel rnam
16a8(rgyud): gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa// sangs rgyas rin chen 'byung ldan gtso// dri la rnam gsum shes byas nas// sangs rgyas sogs la
16b1(rgyud): dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan sna tshogs pa// 'dod chags chos kyi 'byung gnas gtso// ro la rnam gsum shes byas nas/ lha rnams la ni dbul bar bya// de nyid sangs rgyas sna tshogs pa// 
16b2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thogs med rdo rje 'dzin// reg la rnam gsum shes byas nas// bdag gi rigs la dbul bar bya// de nyid bcom ldan rdo rje can// mi bskyod pa yi tshul brnyes pa'o// gzugs sgra ro la sogs
16b3(rgyud): pa la// rtag tu sems ni sbyar bar bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i snying po bsdus pa'o// gzugs sgra dri sogs sngags pa yis// lha nyid du ni rtag tu sgom// yang na de la sgom
16b4(rgyud): pa ni/ rigs kyi tshul du rnam par sgom// sangs rgyas rjes su dran par sbyor// chos ni rjes su dran sgom pa// sku dang gsung dang thugs rnams sgom// rdo rje rjes su dran sgom pa// rigs ni rjes su
16b5(rgyud): dran par sbyor// khro bo rjes su dran sgom pa// lha ni rjes su dran par sbyor// bsgoms na byang chub thob par 'gyur// bud med gzugs ldan mdangs bzang ba// lo grangs bcu drug lon pa la/ 
16b6(rgyud): byin gyi brlabs kyi gnas gsum gyis// dben par mchod pa rab tu brtsam// de bzhin gshegs pa'i btsun mo'i mchog// spyan la sogs pa bsgom par bya// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyar bas/ 
16b7(rgyud): sangs rgyas dngos grub thob par 'gyur// yi ge hUM dang oM ngag dang // phaT kyang rab tu sgom par bya// 'od zer nam lngas khyab pa yi// pad mo rdo rje bsgom par bya// 'bar bcas zla 'od bzhin du dkar
16b8(rgyud): yid du 'ong ba bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas rjes su dran sbyor la sogs// byang chub 'dod pas bsgom par bya// de la sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na// bA ga la ni ling kha bzhag
17a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas gzugs ni bsgom par bya// ba sku rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas sangs rgyas sprin rnams spro// de la chos rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na// bA ga la ni ling khu
17a2(rgyud): gzhag/ rdo rje chos ni bsgom par bya// ba spu rnams kyi pa ga nas// mkhas pas chos ki sbyin rnams spro// da la rdo dzA rjes su dran pa ji ltar skem zhe na/ bA ga la ni lang kha bzhag/ rdo rje
17a3(rgyud): sems dpa' rnam par sgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// rdo rje sma ni rnams spro bar bya// de la rigs rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ bA ga la ni ling kha bzhag/ sangs rgyas gzugs
17a4(rgyud): ni rab tu sgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas rigs kyi sman rnams spro// de lnga khro bo rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na// bA ga la na ling kha bzhag/ khro bo'i dbang po rab tu
17a5(rgyud): sgom// ba spu rnams kyi bu ga nas// mkhas pas khro bo'i sprin rnams spro// de la dam tshig rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na// bdag gri rdo rje pad mar ldan// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam
17a6(rgyud): sbyar te// rang gi khu ba'i thigs pa yis// sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa'ang mchod// de la dkyil 'khor rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na// dbang po gnyis ni mnyam gzhag ste/ 
17a7(rgyud): mkhas pas rang gi khu ba dag/ rnal 'byor pas ni rtag tu dbyung // dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor tshul du bya// de la sku rdzas su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sku gang yin// pung
17a8(rgyud): po lnga yi rab tu rgyas// sangs rgyas sku yi rang bzhin gyis// bdag kyang de dang 'dra gyur cig/ de la gsung rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ rdo rje chos kyi gsung gang yin// gsung de nges
17b1(rgyud): tshig phun sum tshogs// bdag gi tshig dang de 'dra ste// chos 'dzin pa dang 'dra gyur cig/ de la thugs rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ gsang ba'i bdag po blo ldan pa// kun du bzang po'i
17b2(rgyud): thugs gang yin// rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bur ni// bdag gi sems kyang de 'drar gyur// de la sems can rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ sems can kun gyi sems gang yin// sku dang gsung dang // 
17b3(rgyud): thugs kyi mtshan// de ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// mkha' dang mtshungs par spyod 'gyur cig/ de la sngags thams cad kyi gzugs dang / sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rjes su dran pa ji
17b4(rgyud): ltar sgom zhe na/ sngags kyi rdo rje'i sku gang yin// gsung gis sku yang rnam bsgoms pa// bdag kyang rtag tu de 'dra bar// sngags 'dzin pa dang mnyam gyur cig/ de la dam tshig rjes su dran
17b5(rgyud): pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ khu ba byung ste cho ga bzhin// 'bras bu 'dod pas btung bar bya// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs bsad na// dngos grub rab mchog thob par 'gyur// de la shes rab
17b6(rgyud): kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i dam tshig rjes su dran pa ji lta'o zhe na/ rang bzhin gyis ni 'od gsal ba// thams cad ma skyes zag pa med// byang chub med cing mngon rtogs med// khams kyang med cing
17b7(rgyud): 'byung ba'ang med// de la ma skyes pa rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ thams cad rang bzhin 'od gsal ba// mtshan med mi 'gyur nam mkha' bzhin// gnyis med gnyis su med min zhi// 
17b8(rgyud): shin du dri med nam mkha' bzhin// de la zhe sdang gi rigs la sogs pa'i mchod pa rjes su dran pa ji ltar sgom zhe na/ bud med soms ni rab brtan pa// lo grangs bcu gnyis lo ni rnyed la// rigs
18a1(rgyud): / gyi sbyor bas rab bsgoms te// bdag gi khubs mchod par bya// 'dis ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku// rdo rje 'dzin pa'i thugs dang ni// chos 'dzin mchog gi gsung dag kyang // 
18a2(rgyud): tshe 'di nyid la 'thob par 'gyur// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyang 'grub// gang gzhan phra mor bshad pa rnams/ rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms te// bzlas pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur/ 
18a3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste bdun pa'o// / 
18a4(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dkon mchog dpal gyis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po dbang phyug dam pa/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen
18a5(rgyud): po la bstod pa 'dis gsol ba btab po// rdo rje sems dpa' theg pa che/ nam mkha'i spyod pa rnam spyod pa// kun du bzang po spyod pa'i mchog/ rgyal mchog mchod pa bshad du
18a6(rgyud): gsol// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug che// rdo rje theg pa rab ston pa// namA mkha'i dbyings dang mtshungs pa'i mchog// rgyal gzhi mchod pa bshad du gsol// thar pa'i lam ni rab/ 
18a7(rgyud): ston pa// theg pa gsum gyi lam la gnas// sangs rgyas skal mchog dag pa'i bdag/ mi mchog mchod pa bshad du gsol// byang chub sems ni rgyas pa'i spyan/ chos kyi 'khor
18a8(rgyud): lo rab bskor ba// sku dang gsung thugs shin du dag/ phyag 'tshal rdo rje theg pa la'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// thams cad nam mkha' mi 'gyur che// thams cad dbang bskur kun
18b1(rgyud): gyi don// kun dbang rdo rje rin chen 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod pa'i mchog/ rdo rje mi phyed gsum gnas pa// sku dang gsung dang thugs skal mchog/ rgyal ba 'byung bar 'gyur
18b2(rgyud): pa bshad// na chung gzhon nu mig yangs pa// gzugs bzang gzhon pas brgyan pa ni// lo grangs nyi shu lnga lon rnyed// byol song las kyang rab tu brtag/ sa phyogs gtsang zhing rnam par
18b3(rgyud): dben pa'am// rgyal nyid skyos zhi zhi ba'i gnas rnams su// gshang gci tshu la sogs pas byug pa'am// rgyal ba mchod phyir rtag par rab tu bya// nu ma'i dbus par spyi gtsug mtha'
18b4(rgyud): yi bar// cho ga shes pas yang na rkang pa'i bar// lte ba rked pa gsang ba rgyal ba'i sras// rig lnga rnams ni dgod par rab tu bya// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// ye shes
18b5(rgyud): rgya mtsho bsgom par bya// bdag nyid zla ba'i dbus gnas par// mkhas pas snying khar bsgom par bya// zhi ba rdo rje 'dzin 'dod na// bsdu ba dag kyang ragatu bya// rin chen sna bzhi mchod
18b6(rgyud): rten la// 'od zer phreng bas rnam par rgyan// ye shes rgya mtsho dus gsum gyi// gnas te yin por rnam par bsam// bdag gi ba spu'i bu ga nas// mkhas pas mchod pa'i sprin
18b7(rgyud): rnams spro// mkhas pas ud pa la ngag dang // pad ma rnam pa lngar shes bya// dza ti rnam gsum shes byas nas// lha rnams la nI dbul bar bya// me tog dkar ni ka ra dang // ma la
18b8(rgyud): ka dang yu ti ki/ me tog ka ra bai rar bsam// mchod par thams cad rab tu rtag/ dpag tshad brgya yi khyon tsam du// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor sgom byas la// rnam par mkhas pas
19a1(rgyud): brtag par ni// rigs rnams rab tu dgod par bya// de bzhin pad mo rdo rje dang // ral gri ud pa la mkhas pas sgom/ dpag tshad bye ba'i khyon tsam la// / gru bzhi
19a2(rgyud): shin du mdzes pa yi// mchod rten rin chen sna bzhi pa// gsol zhing rung bzhin dri ma med// rigs rnams thams cad mchod pa'i phyir// shes rab can gyi gnas su sgom// 'dod
19a3(rgyud): pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis// de la mchod pa rgya mtsho brtsam// rin chen na bza' la sogs pas// byang chub 'dod pas brtag tu mchod// mchod pa rnam lnga mchog rnams kyis// 
19a4(rgyud): rtag tu lha rnams mnyes par bya// rin chen 'byung gnas na cung mchog/ rin chen sna tshogs mchog gis pa rgyan// bsgrubs tshe rab tu 'grub pa'i phyir// sangs rgyas kun la dbul bar
19a5(rgyud): bya// zhing 'di rin chen sna bdun gyis// mkhas pa dag gis yongs bkang la// dngos grub 'dod pas sbyin pa'i phyir// nyin re shes rab can gyis dbul// bdag po'i phyag rgyar mnyam
19a6(rgyud): gzhag la// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus drag tu// 'dod chags blo can sangs rgyas la// reg pa'i sbyor ba dbul bar bya// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// dkyil
19a7(rgyud): 'khor bkod pa bsgom par bya// de bzhin gshegs pa bdag gi lus// bla ma gshang dang gci bas mchod// bzhin bzongs shin du mdzes po yi// na chung skal ba mchog ldan pa/ 
19a8(rgyud): byin gyis brlabs kyis gnas bsams te// sangs rgyas mchod pa rab tu brtag// mig bzangs brtan pa'i blo ldan pa// khu ba blangs nas bza' bar bya// 'di ni sngags rnams
19b1(rgyud): thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi mchod pa ste// ye shes rdo rje can gyi gsang // sngags rnams dngos grub byed par gsungs// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
19b2(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba// gsang ba 'dus pa las/ gshang gci'i dam tshig gi le'u ste brgyad pa'o// / de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin/ 
19b3(rgyud): thams cad nam mkha' mi 'gyur che// thams cad dbang bskur spyod pa'i mchog/ dbang phyug dam pa kun don gyis// sku gsung thugs la longs spyod pa// rdo rje mi phyed gsum dkyil
19b4(rgyud): 'khor// sangs rgyas ye shes can gyis gsang // nyams dga' mchog ni rab tu bshad// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rdo rje
19b5(rgyud): mi bskyod rab bsgoms nas// lag tu rdo rje bsgom par bya// 'od 'phro mang po 'bar ba dang // 'od zer sna lngas rab tu gang // dus gsum pa yi sangs rgyas rnams// bsgoms nas
19b6(rgyud): rdo rje phyi mar brlag/ sku gsung thugs kyi longs spyod ni// rdo rjes cher brlag med gyur pa// bsam gtan mchog de snyoms ni ni// thugs kyi dngos grub thob par 'gyur// rdo rje gsang ba 'di lta bus
19b7(rgyud): sems can thams cad bsad na ni// mi bskyod sangs rgyas zhing dag tu// rgyal ba'i sras rnams skye bar 'gyur// 'di ni zhe sdang gi rigs kyi dam tshig de kho na ste// rigs thams cad kyi rgya mtsha
19b8(rgyud): yin par shes par bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// ye shes zer pa rab sgrub pa// ngo bo nyid dag gos pa med// byang chub spyod pa rab ston pas// sangs rgyas byang chub sgrub pa yi// yang
20a1(rgyud): dag dam tshig bka' bstsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rnam par snang mdzad rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas thams
20a2(rgyud): cad rnam par sgom// rin chen kun gyi sbyor ba yis// rdo rje'i gzugs ni rab tu brtag/ nor rnams thams cad phrogs nas su// rdo rdzogasum du rnam bsgoms ni// nor gyi rgya mchos gang ba yi// yid
20a3(rgyud): bzhin nor bu 'dra bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi sras rnams dang // thub pa'i skyes bu mchog tu 'gyur// 'di ni rigs kyi rgya mtsho thams cad las gti mug gi rigs kyi dam tshig yang dag pa nyid du
20a4(rgyud): shes par bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// 'dod chags thar pa rab sgrub pa// gsang ba dag pa dmigs med pa// dkyil 'khor rab tu bka' bstsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas
20a5(rgyud): par// pad mo'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// dpag med tshe ni rab bsgoms la// sangs rgyas rnams kyis thams cad dgang // bud med lta bur sbyar ba ni// dam tshig bzhi yi sbyor ba yis// thams
20a6(rgyud): cad de ru bsgom par bya// 'di ni rdo rje tshul mchog go// dbu po gnyis ni rab sbyor bas// de dag thams cad nye bar spyod// 'di ni rdo rje thams cad kyi// mi phyed sku gsum sgom pa'o// 'di ni 'dod
20a7(rgyud): chags kyi yang dag po'i dam tshig ste// sngags pa rnams kyis bsgom par bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sngags kyi don sgrub pa// bdag med ye shes las byung bas// gsung ni
20a8(rgyud): 'di skad bka' bstsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// rdo rje thogs med rab bsgoms te// sangs rgyas thams cad bsgom par
20b1(rgyud): bya/ thams cad gzugs su rnam bsgoms nas// rdo rje tshig gi brdzun smra ngas// rgyal ba kun gyi gnas rnams dang // rgyal ba thams cad bsgru bar bya// 'di na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// nam
20b2(rgyud): mkhwa'i gsung ste dri med pa// ye shes blo can kun gyi gsang // sngags kyi dngos grub thob par bshad// 'di ni dam tshig 'gugs pa'i rigs kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid de// dron ji lta ba
20b3(rgyud): bzhin du spro bar bya'o// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje pa mi phyed gsum rgyal gnas// rdo rje dngos grub rab ston pas// gsung ni 'dri skad bka' bstsal to// nam mkhya' dbyings kyi
20b4(rgyud): dbus gnas par// dam chog dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// dkon mchog dpal na ra ba bsgoms te// gzugs rnams kun gyis 'di dag dgang // rtsub pa'i ngag la sogs po ni// bstan
20b5(rgyud): na ye shes thob par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje bkod pas// de skad ces bka' bstsal to// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam
20b6(rgyud): tshig rdo rje dpal la sogs pa'i// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur cing // rmad du gyur nas/ rdo rje'i tshig 'di smras so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
20b7(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi bdag po// khams gsum las 'das shing // 'jig rten thams cad las 'das pas// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi 'khor
20b8(rgyud): gyi nang du 'di lta bu'i yang dag pa ma yin pa'i tshig gi lam/ rdo rje'i tshig 'di ci'i slad du gsung // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis brjod kyis mi lang bI yA brjod
21a1(rgyud): kyis mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi ri rab kyi rdul phra mo snyed kyi// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dam tshig gi rdo rje dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de
21a2(rgyud): dag la 'di skad ces bka bskul to// rigs kyi bu dman pa'i 'du shes dang / smad pa'i 'du shes 'di lta bu ma bskrad cig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ sngags kyi spyod
21a3(rgyud): pa ni spyod pa'i mchog go// 'di lta ste/ sngags kyi spyod pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na/ nam mkha' ni thams cad kyi rjes su song ba ste// chos
21a4(rgyud): thams cad kyang nam mkha'i khongs su gtogs pa'o// chos de dag thams cad kyang 'dod pa'i khams na mi gnas/ gzugs kyi khams na mi gnas/ gzugs med pa'i khams na mi
21a5(rgyud): gnas// 'byung ba chen po bzhi po la yang mi gnas so// rigs kyi bu chos thams cad kyang de ltar rjes su rig par bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni don gyi dbang 'di lta bu mkhyen cing
21a6(rgyud): sems can rnams kyi bsam pa mkhyen nas// chos 'chad par mdzad do// rigs kyi bu de ltar nam mkha'i tshig nges par brjod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dam tshig de dag rjes su
21a7(rgyud): rig par bya'o// rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste/ dper na/ rtsub shing dang rtsub stan dang / mi'i lag pa bskyod pa'i rkyen gyis du ba myur du byung zhing / me 'byung bar 'gyur mod kyi/ me de
21a8(rgyud): yang rtsub shing la yang mi gonas/ rtsubasnyan la yang mi gnas/ ma'i lag pa bskyod pa la yang mi gnas so// de lta bu'i rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i
21b1(rgyud): dam tshig 'gro ba dang 'ong ba la sogs pa rjes su rig par bya'o// de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur nas/ rngam zhing gdangs te/ tshig 'di skad ces smras so// rmad
21b2(rgyud): 'byung chen po'i chos rnams ni/ nam mkha' dang ni mtshungs pa dang // rnam par mi rtog dag pa las// kun rdzob tu yang bshad pa 'tshar// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
21b3(rgyud): thugs kyi gas dra ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa lus/ don dam pa'i theg pa de kho na nyid kyi dam tshig gi le'u ste dgu pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams
21b4(rgyud): cad yang 'dus te/ bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po rdo rje de kho na nyid mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa/ sku dang gsung dang thugs gsang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phyag 'tshal te/ 'di
21b5(rgyud): skad ces gsol to// de nyid sngags snying kun bsdus pa// sku dang gsung thugs gsang bar bsgrags// dngos grub chen po tshul gyi mchog/ yang dgra bcom ldan bshad du gsol// de nas rgyal
21b6(rgyud): po rdo rje 'dzin// nyon mongs kun gyi rgya mchogatso// 'bar ba drag po skyon yongs pas// gsung ni 'di skad bka' bstsal to// lus dang ngag dang yid rnams ni// rnam par mi rtog mi dmigs
21b7(rgyud): pa// gang na'ang mi gnas mnyam pa nyid// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje sgom// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rang bzhin gyis dag pas pha rol du phyin pa sngags kyi tshul rdo rje zhes
21b8(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad rnal 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mi bskyod
23a1(rgyud): pa la sogs pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rig pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dang thabs gcig tu sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba la rol pa ston par mdzad de// 
23a2(rgyud): phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' klas par 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams kyis rol cing 'gyed la yongs su spyod pa yod kyang / de dag sngags spyod pa la mngon par brtson pa rnam
23a3(rgyud): l-i/ kye ma 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sngags kyi spyod pa'i tshul gyis chos rdzogs par gyur to snyam nas spyan ras kyis mi 'tsho ste/ de bas na skyes bu dam pa de rnams la
23a4(rgyud): spyan ras kyis btsa ba'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i sngags kyi gsang ba/ sngags thams cad kyi snying po kun du bskul bar byed pamra
23a5(rgyud): zhes bya ba rab tu gsang po/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dam tshig la dmigs pa/ rdo rje 'dzin thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dadang thugs kyi drim
23a6(rgyud): tshig l-i dmigs pa/ chos 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung da'i thugs kyi dam tshig la dmigs pa 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje la sa tshig gi lam nges par brjod pas
23a7(rgyud): sngags bsdus pa 'di lta bu gsungs so// / hUM oM ai swA hA/ de nas 'di ni gsungs tsam gyis// sangs rgyas sras dang bcas pa kun// rab tu 'dar zhing rgyal bar 'gyur/ 
23a8(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' rjes su dran// de nas phyag na rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos dam tshig 'di gsungs so// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// 
23b1(rgyud): bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de yi dbus gnas yi ge hUM// rang gizugs su rab tu brtag/ rdo rje'i 'od zer cher 'bar ba// rnam par 'phro bas bsam par bya// sangs rgyas
23b2(rgyud): kyi sku gsung thugs// drungs par de yis rnam bsgoms na// de ma thag tu de 'gyur ba// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// kun gyi gtso bo dbang phyug mchog
23b3(rgyud): rang gi dkyil 'khor rang rdo rjes// bskyed par byed pa'i tshul du 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// snying po rdo rje bsdus pa yin// rang sngags skyes bu bsgoms nas ni// gnas
23b4(rgyud): bzhi rnams su gzugs kyi tshul// zhol gsum lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// kha dog gsum du rab tu sgom// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje dam tshig gis// de skad ces bka' bstsal to// de la 'di ni
23b5(rgyud): rdo rje mchog gi gsang ba'o// snying kha'i dbus su phra mo yis// dkyil 'khor rnams ni bsam par bya// yig mchog tu gyur pa'i tshig// de yi dbus su bsam par bya// rdo rje chen po rtse lnga
23b6(rgyud): pa/ rtag tu sbyor bas bsgom par bya// rdo rje kyo bo'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje gsum rnams bsgom par bya// de yas snying khar brdab bya ste// lha rnams rab tu bskul bar bya// 'di ni rdo rje thams
23b7(rgyud): cad kyi// sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa'o// rdo rje pad mo'i rigs la sogs// rdo rje kyo ba rnam sgom zhing // snying kha ru ni bskul bar bshad// 'di ni rol mo'i 'byung ba ste// rdo rje yi ni
23b8(rgyud): tshul mchog 'di// zhag bdun par du byas na ni// ye shes rdo rje can gyi gsang // sku dang gsung thugs 'grub par 'gyur// mechog stsol ba dag rnam par gzigs// yid ni 'jigs shing / 
24a1(rgyud): skrag gyur nas// yid la mgu zhing dga' 'gyur ba'i// dngos grub rgya chen ster bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams// sngags kyi spyod pa'i mchog 'grub pas
24a2(rgyud): rmongs pas 'da' bar byas na ni// de yi srog ni der zad 'gyur// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje gsum gyi ston pa mchog/ 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtses// gsung ni 'di skad bka'
24a3(rgyud): bstsal to// sngags kyi sgras bu ji snyed pa// rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes rdzogs// dbang po gnyis kyi sbyor ba yis// dngos po thams cad brtag par bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sngags
24a4(rgyud): kyi dam tshig sgom pa'o// rig ma dbang phyug zhugs pa la// rdo rje'i sbyor ba rab sgom zhing // chags la chags pas blta bar bya// 'di ni dam tshig dkyil 'khor ro// de nas rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// 
24a5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi sras// thams cad dbang bskur sangs rgyas gtses// gsung ni 'di skad bka' bstsal to// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad na// bud myed ji snyed yod pa kun// 
24a6(rgyud): phyag rgya che sogs sbyor ba yis// de dag thams cad nye bar spyod// bye ba grangs med rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas gnas ni der sbyor bya// bcom ldan 'das byang chub kyi dam tshig gis de skad bka'
24a7(rgyud): bstsal to// rdo rje gsum po mkha' 'dra ba'i// byang chub 'di yis thob par 'gyur// byang chub sems dpa' rgyal rgya mtsho// rdo rje sems dpa'i tshe des thob// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
24a8(rgyud): kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba/ gsang ba 'dus pa las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po bskul ba zhes bya ba'i le'u ste ban pa'o// / 
24b1(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i skyes bu mchog ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ 
24b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags rdo rje rig pa'i skyes bu'i le'u 'dri gsungs so// rdo rje gsum yi ge sngags kyi mchog/ phyag rgya chen po rnam sgom pa// byang chub thams cad 'thob pa'i
24b3(rgyud): phyir// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// oM ni ye shes snying po ste// rdo rje swA ni thob byed pa'o// a ni byang chub bdag me pa'o// rdo rje'i gsung ni 'thob byed pa'o// hUM ni sku gsung thugs yin te// rdo rje
24b4(rgyud): mi phyed gsum thob pa'o// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi skyes bus/ de skad ces bka' bstsal to// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus gnas par/ 
24b5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor rdo rje kun skye bsam// rdo rje sprin ni 'phro bskyed pa// de ru yi ge b+h+rUM bsam mo// de la 'di ni ye shes rdo rje snying po b+h+rUM// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// oM zhes bya ba rab tu
24b6(rgyud): sgom// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// yi ge A ni bsgom par bya// chos kyi 'khor lo dbus gnas par// yi ge hU~M ni rab tu sgom// yi ge b+huM ga gnas bsgoms te// rdo rje
24b7(rgyud): gsum 'byung bsgom par bya// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig gsang bas de skad bka' bstsal to// snying po dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi// sku gsung thugs ni mnyes byed pa// oM ni sangs rgyas
24b8(rgyud): sku yi mchog/ oM A ni sangs rgyas gsung gi lam// aHhUM ni thugs kyi ye shes 'dzings// hU~M/ byang chub tshul mchog 'di yin te// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sangs rgyas
25a1(rgyud): / byang chub ra bsgrub pa// ye shes rdo rje sprul pa ste// sangs rgyas rgyu dang 'bras bu 'byung // 'di dag sangs rgyas skyes bu ste// sngags kyi rig pa zhes kyang grags// rdo rje mi phyed
25a2(rgyud): gsum bsgoms pa'i// dam tshig dag gis rdzogs par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid kyi ye shes rdo rje byin gyis rlob pa
25a3(rgyud): dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// dben zhing rab tu nyams dga' bar// spror pa 'di ni kun brtsams nas// rdo rje sku dang gsung dang thugs// zla ba phyed kyis nges par 'grub// gsal bI
25a4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha'i rdo rje dbus bsams te// rang gi sngags kyi dam tshig bskyed// yi ge e na snying khar bzhag/ 'od zer lA yi sprin chen po// rnam par snang mdzad mchog
25a5(rgyud): rluta sgom// 'di yis sangs rgyas rnams kyi s+ya// rdo rje rnam snang rgya mtshor 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan bsnyen na ni// sangs rgyas sku ni 'dra ba'i mdog/ rdo rdza bskal pa gsum du gnas// zla ba
25a6(rgyud): phyed kyis 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das sku rdo rje gsang bas de skad ces bka' bsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku rdo rje 'od zer bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 
25a7(rgyud): chos kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha'i rdo rje dbus su bsam// rang gi sngags kyis skyes bu bskyed// a ni ngag gi lam bzhag ste// kha tog lnga pa'i pad ma chi// 'jug rten dbang
25a8(rgyud): mchog sgom pa yis// dam tshig ye shes rdzogs byas te// tshig gi dam tshig lnga yi mchog/ chos kyi tshig gi lam gnas pa// rdo rje chos dang mtshungs par 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan
25b1(rgyud): bsten na ni// rdo rje bskal bya gsum du gnas// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsung gsang bas de skad ces bka' bskul to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung rdo rje'i dam tshig 'byung ba zhe
25b2(rgyud): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus su bsam// rang sngags skyes bu rdzogs byas la// sems la yi ge hU~M gnas pa// dam tshig chen po 'di nyid ni// kha dog
25b3(rgyud): rnam lngar bsgom par bya// rdo rje kun dang rgyal ba'i gnas// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// ston pa rdo rje thugs 'dra ba// ye shes yon tan rgya mtshor 'gyur// ye shes lnga ldan bstan na ni// rdo rje bskal pa
25b4(rgyud): gsum du gnas// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje'i thug bas de skad bka' bstsal to// de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// ye shes
25b5(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dbus su ni// rdo rje chen po bsgom par bya// lus rnams kun la khung dmigs na// rdo rje ye shes mkha' mnyam 'gyur// khaM/ sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yis// yang dang yang du
25b6(rgyud): mchod pa dang // bskal pa gsum du dam tshig gnas// sangs rgyas kyis kyang gzigs mi 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das nam mkha' rdo rje dam tshig gis de skad ces bka' bstsal to// sku dang gsung dang thugs
25b7(rgyud): rdo rje mi snang ba 'byung ba bkod pa phreng ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor dbus su ni// rang sngags skyes bur rab bsams la// snying khar rdo rje hU~M zhes pa// bzhag ste 'od zer rnam par
25b8(rgyud): sgom// 'jam dpal mtshig longs spyod pa// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// sa bcu dag lnga gnas pa yi// byang chub sems dpar de 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi dmatshig
26a1(rgyud): rdo rje zla ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 'od zer 'bar ba'i yi ge TI// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su bsam// mtshon mchog rdo rje'i lus ngag gis// rdo rje'i sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur
26a2(rgyud): shrI nam mkha'i rdo rje dam tshig gi bkod pa'i gnas zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// sangs rgyas mngon shes dam tshig mchog/ rdo rje 'chang dang 'dra bar 'gyur// 'di ni dngos grub thams cad kyi/ 
26a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas mngon shes mchog bsgrub pa'o// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje sems dpa' rab bsgoms la// nam mkha'i dbyings
26a4(rgyud): kyi dbus gnas par// ye shes oM ni bsgom par bya// oMrdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pa// mi bskyod rdo rje gsum 'drar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi bskyod pas// de skad ces
26a5(rgyud): bka' bstsal to// mi bskyod pa yi sku 'dra dang // gsung dang thugs mchog 'dra bar 'dzin// 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad du// mi bskyod rdo rjes mchod par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das
26a6(rgyud): rdo rje mi bskyod pa'i sku dang mnyam pa mngon par 'byung ba'i dam tshig rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor 'od bzang bsam// nam
26a7(rgyud): mkha'i rdo rje rab bsgrims la// rin chen oM ni bsam par bya// e/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas// rdo rje gsum gyi dpal 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// dkon
26a8(rgyud): mchog dpal gyi 'od dang 'dra// de ni bdag med byang chubo dang // ye shes gsang ba 'dra gnas 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dkon mchog dpal gyis de skad bka'
26b1(rgyud): bstsal to// rin po che'i ljongs spyod do rje dam tshig longs spyod rdo rje'i tshul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pA bsam// 'jig
26b2(rgyud): / rten dbang phyug rab bsgoms la// chos kyi o ni bsgom par bya// oM/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas// rdo rje gsum dpag med 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yi// 'od dpag
26b3(rgyud): med dang 'dre bar 'gyur// de ni sems can thams cad kyi// theg chen las ni 'byung bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'od dpag med pas de skad bka' bstsal to// yon tan dpag tu med
26b4(rgyud): pa rdo rje ni 'od kyi dpal ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje ud pa la bsgoms pa// dam tshig oM ni ra ba tu
26b5(rgyud): sgom// ai/ rdo rje dam tshig gsum bsgoms pas// rdo rje gdon mi zo 'drar 'gyur// lus dang ngag sems rdo rje yis// rdo rje thogs med 'dra ba'i 'od// de na dpal ldan ye shes mtsho// sem/ 
26b6(rgyud): can kun don 'byung bar 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gdon mi za bas de skad bka' bstsal to// gdon mi za'i dam tshig 'od zer gyi ye shes kyi mchog 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 
26b7(rgyud): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus su ni// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dam pa bsam// rdo rje snang mdzad rab bsgoms la// sku gsung oM ni rab tu sgom// oM/ rdo rje dam tshig rab bsgoms pas/ 
26b8(rgyud): rnam par snang mdzad mnyam par 'gyur// lus dang ngag yid rdo rje yis// rnam par snang mdzad 'dra ba'i 'od// de ni ye shes rdzogs byang chub// sku gsum mi phyed sgrub byed 'gyur// bcom
27a1(rgyud): ldan 'das rnam par snad mdzad kyis de skad ces bka' bstan to// lus dang ngag ying dmigs pa mngon par byang chub pan tshe zhes bya bya'i ting du 'dzin to// rnam pa
27a2(rgyud): dang // rlung dang 'brub rgyu rnams dang ni// dur gyi drod la stsogs par yang // bsamya gtan bsdus pa 'di dag sgros// mi bskyod ye shes dag lo sogs// rdo rje nam mkha'i dkyil du byas ma// 
27a3(rgyud): mngon shes lnga pa'i sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas mchog gi gnas sgom// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po rdo rje mngon por mkhyen pas de skad bka' bsngal to// rdo rje chen po ts+tsha lnga pA/ 
27a4(rgyud): 'bar ba lnga yis rnam par rgyan// gnas lnga dag tu sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mngon shes 'dra bar 'gyur// me stag mang po 'khrug po yi// rang sngags 'khor lo bsgom par bya// rdo rje lnga yi
27a5(rgyud): sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mngon shes 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje nam mkha'i dkyil nyid du// 'khor lo sangs rgyas 'bar 'od 'dra// sangs rgyas 'jug par rab bsgoms nas// sangs rgyas
27a6(rgyud): gnas dang 'dra bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// bdag gi lus la maM snang mdzad gzhag/ snying khar yi ge oM bsams la// sngags la rnam par shes pa sgom// 
27a7(rgyud): 'gog pa'i rdo rje sems nyid du// gang tshe de las skyes gyur na// sangs rgyas kun gyi mchog 'dzin pa// yid bzhin dpal ldan lta burdzu 'gyur// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par
27a8(rgyud): rdo rje mi skyong rab tu sgom/ snying khar yi ge hUM bsgoms nas// sems ni thig ler gyur par gzhag/ sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// tshe dpag med par rab tu sgom/ 
27b1(rgyud): snying khar yi ge a bsams te// rdo rje thig ltar gyur par gzhag/ 'di de dam tshig mchog gtso yin// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pa// 'gog pa'i dam tshig ye shes te// sangs rgyas dngos grub
27b2(rgyud): tho ba 'gyur ba'o// rdo rje nam mkha'i dbyings gnas par// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// lus ngag sems la yi ge oM// bsams na do ni bskal par gnas// rdo rje nam mkha'i
27b3(rgyud): dbyings gnas par// chos kyi dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// lus ngag sems la aM yi ge a// bsams na de ni bskal bar gnas// rdo rngonam mkha' dbyings gnas par// rdo rjod dkyil
27b4(rgyud): 'khor bsgom par bya// lus ngag sems la yig hUM// bsams na de ni bskal bar gnas// bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsum gyi tog ni tshig gis de skad bka' bstsal to// skra dang gsung dang thug
27b5(rgyud): rdo rje yi// rnal 'byor 'dir gyur phyin chad ni// klog gam yang na sems kyang rung // de yang rdo rje 'dzin 'drar 'gyur// de bzhini gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba
27b6(rgyud): gsang ba 'dus pa las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sngags kyi dam tshig de kho na nyid rdo rje rig pa'i skyes bu'i mchog gi le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o/ 
27b7(rgyud): de nas skyon po rdo rje 'dzin// bskyed pa ye shes mchog sgrub pa// dmachog de nyid rdo rje gsum// rdo rje gsung gis bka' bsngal bapa// nim mkha' mtshungs par mnyam gyur pa// rnam
27b8(rgyud): mi rtog ngo bo nyid// chos rnams rang bzhin dag pa la// rol mo 'di dag rab tu sgom// dgon pa chen po'i sa phyogs sam// me tog 'bras bu sogs pas rgyan// ri bong ben pa'i sa phyog su
28a1(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad bsdus pas 'grub// mAM/ lus dang ngag sems rdo rje la// rdo rje 'jam pa rab tu sgom// lus dang ngag sems las smos pas// rdo rje 'jam pa 'dra bar 'gyur
28a2(rgyud): dpag tshad brgya'i khyon tsam du// rdo rje 'bar ba 'od dag gis// rgyan rnams kun gyis brgyan pa yi// dag pa'i bdag nyid snang bar 'gyur// tshangs pa drag po la sogs lhas// nams kyang
28a3(rgyud): mthong bar ma 'gyur ro// rdo rje 'jam pa mchog gi dam tshig mi snang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje mi phyed gsum las phyung // gshang la gci dam tshig lnga rnams ni// lcags gsum las
28a4(rgyud): byung ldan byas te// khar bcug nas ni bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas kun gyi mi phyed pa// thugs na de ru rab bsgoms na// rdo rje 'jam pa'i 'od 'dra bar// de ma thag tu de 'gyur ro// 'khor lo 'od
28a5(rgyud): 'phro mdangs mchog can// rang gi sngags kyis rab bsgoms nas// sangs rgyas thams cad bzhugs pa'i gnas// bsgoms na sangs rgyas 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gi// 
28a6(rgyud): rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// rdo rje 'dzin dang 'dra ba kun// de yi rjes su 'brang bar 'gyur// 'khor lo dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// rdo rje chen po rang sngags kyis// dkyil 'khor dbus su
28a7(rgyud): rab bsgoms la// rdo rje kun gyi gnas yin par// bsams na rdo rje 'dra bar 'gyur// ri rab sum bcu rtsa drug gi// rdul phran jiHyod paHyi// de snyed kyi ni bud med rnams// yon tan can gyi
28a8(rgyud): gnas su gyur// drag po dag gis phyag byas pa// khams gsum rdo rje chen por 'gyur// rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// pad ma chen po mdapa brgyad pa// rang sngags rdo rje
28b1(rgyud): bsams nas su// chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin par// bsams na chos dang 'dra bar 'gyur// / ri rab su ma bcu rtsa drug gi// rdul phran ji snyed yod pa yi// sangs rgyas mchod mchog
28b2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor du// dag pa'i bdag nyid 'jog par byed// pad mo mnyam pa nyid ces bya ba'i ting 'dzin to// ye shes lnga ldan rab bsnyen na// bskal pa gsum gyi yun du gnas// phyogs bcu
28b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba gsum la bsnyen bkur byed// 'od zer lnga'i mdog 'dra'i 'od// rang gi sngags kyi ral gri sgom// mig yangs lag na thogs na ni// rdo rje gsumo rig
28b4(rgyud): 'dzin par 'gyur// khams gsum kun gyis rab mchod cing // tshangs dbang lha min phyag byas pa// stong gsum na ni gcig pu dpa'// mi mchog gsang ba 'dzin par 'gyur// gang rnams
28b5(rgyud): 'dod dang bsams pa dag/ sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'dzin// rdo rje thugs las rab tu phyung // de lta bu yi dngos grub ster// ral gri thams cad kyi dam pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// oM
28b6(rgyud): ni ri lu tsa na ka'i// 'bru tshad tsam du bsams nas ni// dbus su rang gi lce yi gzugs// bsams te khar bcug rnams bsgoms na// de ni de ma thag tu yang // byang chub ye shes 'od 'drar
28b7(rgyud): 'gyur// nyi ma shar ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // 'dzam bu'i chu bo gser gyi mdog// a ni ra lu tsa na ka'i/ 'bru tshad tsam du bsams nas ni// dbus su rang gi lha yi gzugs// bsams te kha
28b8(rgyud): bcug rnam bsgoms na// de ni de ma thag tu yang // byang chub ye shes 'od 'drar 'gyur// nyi ma shar ba'i 'od 'dra zhing // 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser gyi mdog// hU~M ni ri lu tsa na ka'i// 'bru tshad tsam/ 
29a1(rgyud): du bsams nas ni// dbus su rang gi lha yi gzugs// bsams te khyur bcug rnam bsgoms sa// d+he nI de mthug tu yang // rdo rje srung nga 'od 'drar 'gyur// mkha' dbyings
29a2(rgyud): gsal ba'i dkyil gnas par// rnam par snang mdzad rab tu sgom// lag tu 'khor lo rab bsgoms na// 'khor lo'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// 'khor lo chen po'i rigs bsgoms te/ 
29a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas skur ni rab sbyor zhing // ye shes 'di ni rab sgrub pa// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// mkha' dbyings rdo rje'i dbus gnas par// ye shes mi bskyod rab bsgoms te// lag tu rdo rje rab
29a4(rgyud): bsgoms na// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rdo rje chen po'i rigs bsgoms te// rdo rje skur ni rab sbyor zhing // rdo rje mchog 'di sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// mkha' dbyings rin
29a5(rgyud): chen dbus gnas par// rin chen rdo rje rab tu sgom// lag tu rin chen rab bsgoms na// rin chen rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// rin po che'i rigs bsgoms na// rin chen skur ni ri ba
29a6(rgyud): sbyor zhing // rin chen mchog 'di sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// mkha' dbyings chos kyi dbus gnas par// tshe dpag med pa rab tu sgom// lag tu pad mo rab bsgoms na// 
29a7(rgyud): pad mo'i rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// pad ma'i rigs chen bsgoms nas su// chos kyi skur ni rab sbyor zhing // pad mo'i mchog 'di sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya// mkha'
29a8(rgyud): dbyings dam tshig dbus gnas par// gdon mi zla ba'i ye shes bsgoms// lag tu ral gri rab bsgoms na// ral gri rig pa 'dzin par 'gyur// dam tshig chen po'i rigs bsgoms
29b1(rgyud): te/ thogs med dam tshig rab sbyor zhing // dam tshig mchog ni sgrub pa ni// ye shes rdo rje dag gis bya/ rtse gsum ye shes ljags kyu sogs// rdo rje khyad par gyis bsgrubs na// sku gsung
29b2(rgyud): thugs kyi sgrub pa yis/ bsam gtan des ni 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig chen po'i dngos grub rdo rjes de skad bka' bstsal to// lam kyi bzhi mdo 'am shing gcig drung / 
29b3(rgyud): mtshan ma gcig dang zhi gnas su// rdo rje dgug pa'i khyad par gyis// sgrub pa pos ni rtag tu sgrub// sbyor gsum rdo rje can rnams kyis// sbyor gsum sngags kyi skyes bu bsam/ 
29b4(rgyud): sangs rgyas ye shes blo ldan gyi// sku gsung thugs kyi kyo ba btang // rlung gi dkyil 'khor mchog gnas par// sangs rgyas dgug pa dam pa yin// dam tshig las byung phyogs bcu pa/ 
29b5(rgyud): rdo rjes bkug nas nye bar spyod// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dam tshig rdo rje 'gugs pa'i cho ga'o// rnam par snang mdzad 'khor lo che// rdo rje pad mo la sogs pas// rgyal gnas lcags
29b6(rgyud): kyu bsams nas ni// dam tshig dgug chog kyo ba bya/ khams gsum gyi dam tshig dgug pa'o// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas sku ni rnam bsgoms la/ 
29b7(rgyud): log tu sku dang gsung thugs kyi// kye be la sogs rab tu sgom// 'di dag lta bu'i sbyor ba yi// de ni gnas las byed par 'gyur// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// rdo rje sku ni
29b8(rgyud): rnams bsgoms la// rdo rje'i sbyor ba lce bsgoms na// rdo rje gsung dang 'dra bar 'gyur// rnam pa mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sangs rgyas skur na rnam bsgoms la// lag
30a1(rgyud): tu sgrub bya bsams nas ni// rdo rje dang ni 'dra bar 'gyur// gsang gsum dam tshig mchod pa'i mchog/ mchod pas mchod na sna rab tu sgrub// 'di ni sangs rgyas
30a2(rgyud): thams cad kyi// gsang ba'i snying po bsdus pa yin// bcom ldan 'das gsang ba chen po'i dam tshig gis de skad gsungs so// sha chen dam tshig mchog gis ni// rdo rje gsung
30a3(rgyud): mchog sgrub par bya// gshang gci dam tshig mchog gis ni// rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bor 'gyur// glang po'i sha yi dam tshig gis// mngon shes lnga dag thob par 'gyur// rta
30a4(rgyud): dag gi dam tshig gis// mi snang ba yi bdag por 'gyur// khyi sha dag gi dam tshig gis// dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// ba lang sha yi dam tshig gis// rdo rje dgug
30a5(rgyud): pa'i mchog tu 'gyur/ sha rnams thams cad med na yang // thams cad bsam pas rnam par brtag/ rdo rje sbyor ba 'di byas na// sangs rgyas thams cad byin gyis rlob// rnam
30a6(rgyud): pa'i mchog rnams kun ldan pa'i// sku dang thugs ni rdo rje can// snying khar ye shes dam tshig dang // dbu rgyan rdo rje mchog 'dzin pa// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyes 'gyur ba// dam
30a7(rgyud): tshig mchog gis bya ba ni// dngos grub thams cad 'grub pa'i mchog/ dam tshig mchog gis rab tu bya// dam tshig sems cad ye shes rdo rjer 'gyur ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
30a8(rgyud): to// lce'i dam tshig rdo rje mchog/ rdo rje can gyi hU~M bsgoms te// bdud rtsi lnga yi sbyor ba yis// zos na rdo rje gsung thob 'gyur// a dang oM gyi dam tshig kyang // 'di ni rdo rje
