30b1(rgyud): tshul mchog ste/ 'di lta bu'i sbyor ba yis// rdo rje mi phyed 'dra bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i dam tshig bdud rtsi'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i ting da rdo rje dam tshig gsum 'grub mchog/ sku
30b2(rgyud): gsum rdo rje can du 'gyur// phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad kyi// nor bu yid bzhin rgya mtshor 'gyur// 'jig rten khams ni thams cad du// rdo rje ba dag nyid snang bar byed/ 
30b3(rgyud): 'khor lo'i dam tshig 'grub pa'i mchog/ sangs rgyas sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur// gang ga'i bye snyed thams cad du// grub pa kun du rnam par spyod// dam tshig dam pa thams cad kyi/ 
30b4(rgyud): rig pa 'dzin pa'i gtso bor 'gyur// rdo rje'i sku ni rab bsgoms pas// thams cad dam chog mchog tu 'grub// mi snang gyur pa thams cad la// slong khams dag ni snang bar byed/ 
30b5(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun las 'phrog pa dang // lha yi bu mo mchog la spyod// gang gA'i bye snyed sangs rgyas rnams// rdo rje gsum gyi gnas bzhugs pa// rang lag skyu ru ra bzhag bzhin// rdo rje mig
30b6(rgyud): gis mthong bar 'gyur// gang ga'i bye snyed zhing rnams na// sgra drag pa ni ji snyed pa// mngon shes rna bas thos pas ni// rna ba'i drung du 'khod pa bzhin// gang ga'i bye snyed zhing dag gi/ 
30b7(rgyud): sems can kun gyi sems rnams ni// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan pa yi// rol mo las byung sems rig 'gyur// bskal pa gang ga'i bye snyad du// 'khor ba dag na gnos pa yi// sngon gyi
30b8(rgyud): gnas kyi gtan tshogs rnams// zhag gsum len pa bzhin du dran// gang ga'i bye ma snyed kyi lus// sangs rgyas sprin la sogs rgyan pas// bskal pa gang ga'i bye snyed du// rdo rje
31a1(rgyud): 'phrul mchog gis 'gengs// bcom ldan 'das dam tshig mngon par mkhyen pas de skad bka' bskul to// de la mngon par shes pa lnga ni// rdo rje'i spyan dang / rdo rje'i snyan dang / 
31a2(rgyud): rdo rje'i thugs dang / rdo rje'i gnas dang / rdo rje'i rdzu 'phrul lo// sangs rgyas mngon shes lnga don 'grub// sangs rgyas sku dang 'dra bar 'gyur// gang ga'i bya snyed grangs med pa'i// 'khor gyis
31a3(rgyud): yongs su bskor nas su// rdo rje sku dang gsung thugs kyis// 'jig rten khams kun bgrod par 'gyur// bsnyen pa'i dam tshig sbyor ba dang // nye bar sgrub pa 'byung ba dang // sgrub pa'i don gyis
31a4(rgyud): dam tshig dang / sgrub pa chen po dag dang bzhi// rdo rje'i bye brag shes byas la// da nas lam rnams sgrub par bya// bsnyen pa'i ting 'dzin rab sbyor ba// byang chub mchog ni sgom par bya/ nye
31a5(rgyud): bar sgrub pa grub mchog la// rdo rje skye mched rnam par spyad// sngags kyi bdag po bsgoms pa yis// sgrub pa'i tshe na bskul bar gsungs// sgrub pa chen po byed pa'i tshe// rang sngags rdo rje can
31a6(rgyud): gyis gsungs// dbu rgyan la ni bdog po bsam// ye shes rdo rje 'grub par 'gyur// bsnyen pa'i ye shes bdud rtsi dag/ thams cad du na rtag par bya// 'od ni sdigs rnams thams cad kyi/ 
31a7(rgyud): sngags kyi de nyid don grub pa'o// dgon pa chen po'i sa phyogs dang // rab tu rnam par dben pa dang // ri bo nags mdab chu ngogs su// rtag ste dngos grub thob par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das rdo
31a8(rgyud): rje sgrub pa chen pos de skad bka' bstsal to// yang na rdo rje bzhi dag gi/ brtul zhugs brtan pas bsnyen par bya// sku gsum mnyam pa nyid gyur pa// bsgoms na dngos grub 'thob par
31b1(rgyud): 'gyur// dus bzhi drug tu rab sbyor bas// blo dang ldan pas gnas lngar ni// ye shes rdo rje yi ge oM// bsgoms na sdom pa yin par bshad// zhag bdun dang ni zla phyed dang // zla gcig zla ba
31b2(rgyud): phyed dang gnyis// rdo rje dam tshig bsgrubs na ni// dngos grub myur du thob par 'gyur// zhag grangs bye brag rab bskul ba// nga yis rgyas par rab tu bstan// gsang ba mchog las byung ba la// 
31b3(rgyud): zla ba phyed kyis 'grub par gsungs/ de la 'di ni nye bar sgrub pa'i sdom pa'i yul lo// sangs rgyas skyo 'dzin dpal dang ldan// rdo rje mi phyed gsum byed pa// de la sgyu yas mtshan pa ya// byin gyis
31b4(rgyud): brlabs kyi gnas bya ste// rdo rdzing sku dang ldan par bya// mi phyed rdo rje gsum bsgoms pas// phyogs bcu rak+Sha bzhug pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// de la sku yis mtshan pa yi// byin gyi brlabs kyi
31b5(rgyud): gnas mdzad do// de la 'di ni sgrub pa'i sdom pa'i yul lo// chos kyi gsung lam dpal dang ldan// rdo rje mi phyed gsum byed pa// byin gyis brlabs kyi gnas bya ste// rdo rje gsung dang ldan
31b6(rgyud): par bya// rdo rje mi phyed gsum bsgoms pas// phyogs bcu dag na bzhug sangs rgyas// de las gsung las byung ba yi/ Sh+T+r-i/ byin gyi brlabs kyi gnas mdzad do// de la 'di ni sgrub pa chen
31b7(rgyud): po'i sdom pa'i yul lo// rdo rje'i thugs 'dzin dpal dang ldan// rdo rje mi phyed gsum byed pa// byin gyi brlabs kyi gnas bya ste// rdo rje thugs dang ldan par bya// rdo rje mi phyed gsum
31b8(rgyud): bsgoms pas// phyogs na bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams// de yi thugs las byung ba yi// byin gyi brlabs kyi gnas mdzad do// sangs rgyas rdo rje sems dpa' 'am// yang na
32a1(rgyud): chos kyi sems dpa'ang rung // rmongs pas 'da' bar byed na ni// tshal par 'gas par gdon mi za// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang
32a2(rgyud): ba gsang ba 'dus pa las// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i sbyor ba'i dam tshig sgrub pa'i mchog bstan pa'i le'u skye bcu gnyis pa'o// / 
32a3(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan bde gshegs kun// ye shes rdo rje mchog 'dzin pa// sems can kun don yang dag byung // byang chub sems dpe'i blo ldan gyi// thub pa kun don rdo rje can// smyon
32a4(rgyud): pa che la phyag 'tshal nas// dam tshig de nyid mkhyen pa la// mchod de rdo rje dbyings 'di gsungs// e ma'o sangs rgyas tshul re bzang // e ma'o byang chub tshul gyi mchog/ e ma'o chos kyi tshul
32a5(rgyud): re zhi// e ma'o sngags kyi tshul re burtan// ma skyes pa yi chos rnams ni// ngo bo nyid kyi khyad pur can// rnam par mi rtog yang dag las// ye shes 'byung ba rab tu bshad// yid 'ong sngags rnams
32a6(rgyud): kun bsdus pa// rdo rje bzlas pa ye shes che// sku gsum mi phyed dkyil 'khor dang // sangs rgyas ye shes 'thob 'gyur ba// rdo rje ma phyid gsum bsgoms pa'i// rdo rje bzlas pa'i sbyor ba yis
32a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyis byin gyis rlob// rig dang gsang sngags thams cad kyi// sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi mtshan// gsang sngags zlos pa de ring gsungs// ye shes rgya mtsho gsan pa dang // sku
32a8(rgyud): gsung thugs kyi rdo rje can// sangs rgyas dus gsum las byung rnams// rdo rje'i sngags ni rab bsnyems pas// ye shes mnyam med thob gyur pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol/ 
32b1(rgyud): de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// nam mkha' rdo rje ye shes byung // khyed bskyed dam pa mchog gi gtsos// rdo rje bzlas pa 'di gsungs so// sngags kyi don kun bzlas pa ni// rdo rje mi phyed gsum gyis mtshan// rdo rje
32b2(rgyud): dbye ba gsum gyis mthar// bkod pa rdo rje gsum zhes bya// sku gsung thugs kyi gnas rnams su// spro ba rnam pa gsum dag bya// rdo rje bzlas pa 'di yis ni// rdo rje gsum gyi thugs 'drar 'gyur// zhes gsu
32b3(rgyud): so// sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku gsung thugs// bsgoms nas mchod pa'i mchog brtag pa// ye shes rdo rjes byas nas ni// rdo rje gsum gyi thugs 'drar 'gyur// sangs rgyas rnams kyi sku gsung thugs// bsams
32b4(rgyud): nas mchod pa'i mchog brtags pa// ye shes rdo rjes rab tu bya// 'di ni byang chub mchog thob pa'o// yang na dbye ba rnam gsum gyis// so so dag tu spro bar bya// sku dang gsung thugs bdag med par// ye
32b5(rgyud): shes sems kyis yang dag spro// brjod nas rdo rje spro ba ni// rdzogs nas rab tu bsdu bar bya// 'di ni ye shes spyan phye ba// sangs rgyas rnams ni kun gyi yin// sku ni rdo rje rdzogs byang chub// dngos dang dngos
32b6(rgyud): med rnam spyad pa// sangs rgyas sku zhes bya bar bshad// de ni sku yi bzlas par bshad// gsung gi dam tshig rdzogs byang chub// sgra dang sgra min rnam spyad pa// gsung gi rdo rje zhes bshad de// 'di
32b7(rgyud): ni gsung go bzlas par bshad// thugs kyi dam tshig rdzogs byang chub// gnas pa'i rdo rje rnam spyad pa// thugs kyi rdo rje zhes bya ste// de ni thugs kyi bzlas par bshad// don gyi rjes 'gro
32b8(rgyud): bzlas pa yi// ngo bo nyid med bzang po yis// dus gsum sangs rgyas rnam spyad pa// de ni rin chen bzlas par bshad// sangs rgyas zhing rnams thams cad du// sku'i sprin rnams spro ba dang / 
33a1(rgyud): @gzhud cing byon pa'i rdo rje'i gdon// de ni thogs med bzlas par bshad // khro bo'i dam tshig ye shes kyis// rang gi rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor grags// sngags kyi yi ge'i tshig thos pa// de
33a2(rgyud): ni khro bo'i bzlas par bshad// 'dod pa'i don gyis myos gyur pa// kun du stob cing phan par dga'// sems can gti mug gnas la 'jog/ de ni ga mug bzlas par bshad// 'dod chags rdo rje las
33a3(rgyud): byung tshig/ lus dang ngag sems la gnas pa'o// sems can 'dod chags mtshor gnas gzhag/ de ni 'dod chags bzlas par bshad// zhe sdang rdo rje las byung sems// lus dang ngag sems
33a4(rgyud): la gnas pa yi// sems can zhe sdang gnas la gzhag/ de ni zhe sdang bzlas par bshad// dam tshig de nyid rdo rje gsum// dbu ma dam tshig rdo rje can// de nyid dam tshig rdo rje yi// bzlas pa ma ning
33a5(rgyud): zhes bya'o// 'dod chags de nyid don bsgoms pa// rdo rje'i bdag po thams cad ni// sems can kun la phan 'dod pa'i// 'dod chags byang chub rdzogs par mdzad// rig pa chen mo spyan la sogs
33a6(rgyud): rtag tu 'dod pa'i don brtson pa// 'dod pa'i longs spyod dag gis ni// ji ltar 'dod pa bsnyen na 'grub// gti mug dam tshig las byung ba// rig pa'i rgyal po rdo rje can// ma ning dag gi gnas
33a7(rgyud): grub po// dngos grub dam pa rab tu ster// khro bo zhe sdang gnas las skyes// gsod la rtag tu brtson pa dag/ sgrub pa'i mchog gi chos can la// gsod pa'i don gyis 'grub par 'gyur/ 
33a8(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das skyes bu chen po'i dam tshig gis de skad bka' bstsol to// ye shes 'khor lo can rnams kyi// 'khor lo snying kha'i dbus su sgom// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbu
33b1(rgyud): gnas par// dbus su 'khor lo'i don sgom mo// ye shes rdo rje can rnams kyi// rdo rje snying khwa'i dbus su sgom// rdo rjed dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// rdo rje'i sngags don bsgom par bya// rin chen po
33b2(rgyud): shes can rnams kyi// rin chen snying khar dbus su sgrom// rin chen dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// rin chen sngags don sgom par bya// pad ma ye shes can rnams kyi// pad mo snying khe'i dbus su sgom/ 
33b3(rgyud): chos kyi dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// pad mo'i sngags don bsgom par bya// ral gri ye shes can rnams kyi// ral gri s+ya kha'i dbus su sgom// dam tshig dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// ral
33b4(rgyud): gri sngags don bsgom par bya// dkyil 'khor kun gyi ngos rnams su// sangs rgyas lnga rnams dgod par bya// 'od zer lnga yi bye brag gis// spros na byang chub 'thob par 'gyur// sngags rnams

40a1(rgyud): / kha dog dmar po rnam par bsam// rdzogs sangs dpag med dbu brgyan pa// bsgoms nas rdo rje can dag mnyes// 'di ni rdo rje ye shes can// khro bo kun gyi dam tshig can// rta bskyed pa 'byung ba
40a2(rgyud): rnam par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor daM pa ni// nam mkha'i rdo rje dbus su bsam// sangs rgyas gzugs ni rab bsgoms la// rdo rje mi 'chi rab bsgom po// 'bar ba'i
40a3(rgyud): 'od zer dmang po 'gro// rdo rje smin ni kun du 'khrug/ khros shing khro bcas gnag pa dang // mche ba rnon por rab tu sgom// mi bskyod dam tshig dbu brgyan pa// bsgoms na khro bo 'dzin mnyes 'gyur// 'di

40a8(rgyud): 'od zer mang po 'phro// rdo rje gsum gyi gnas dkyil 'khor// khro zhing khros pa zhags pa 'dzin// rdo rje stobs can bsgom par bya// mi bskyod dam tshig dbu brgyan la// bsgoms na rab tu mnyes

40b2(rgyud): rgyas gzugs ni rab gaster+tha A lA// dz+dza sngon po rnam par sgom// gzugs ni rab tu gnag la rno// rgya mtsho nag po bskyed par byed// 'bar ba 'od zer mang po 'phro// rdo rje dbyig thogs sgom par bya// mi bskyod dam/

40b7(rgyud): bsgoms la// rig pa'i 'khor lo rab tu sgom// mtshan rnams thams cad yongs su rdzogs// rdo rje 'bar bas yongs su bskor// gtsug tor 'khor lo bsgyur dam tshig/ rnam par spro ba rab tu sgom/ mi bskyod
40b8(rgyud): dam tshig dbu brgyan la// bsgoms ni rab tu mnyes par 'gyur// 'di ni khro bo thams cad kyi// 'da' bar dka' ba'i dam tshig go/ gtsug tor gyi dam tshig rig pa'i stobs 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i/ 
41a1(rgyud): @ting nge 'dzin to// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha'i rdo rje dbus su bsam// sangs rgyas gzugs ni rab bsgoms la// rdo rje sum b+ha rab tu sgom// me lce rnon po 'bar ba'i sku/ 
41a2(rgyud): rdo rje'i sprin ni rab tu 'phro// phyag na rdo rje rab 'brar ba// bsgoms na dngos grub thob par 'gyur// mi bskyod dam tshig dbu brgyan la// bsgoms na rab tu mnyes par 'gyur// 'di ni khro bo thams cad kyi/ 
41a3(rgyud): 'da' bar dka' ba'i dam tshig go// rdo rje'i dam tshig sum b+ha rab tu 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// 'gog pa khro bo'i 'khor lo ni// sangs rgyas 'khor lo bsten pa yis// ting 'dzin rdo rje ye shes rnams/

41a7(rgyud): ne saR+Wa aR+tha sA d+ha ni swA hA// de nas 'di ni gsungs tsam gyis// 'byor pa kun la dgyes pa rnams// mnyes shing rab tu dgyes gyur nas// sangs rgyas rdo rjes rjes su dran// sangs rgyas rnams kyi zhi 'byung ba// las rnams

41b1(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje 'dzin thams cad kyi btsun mo'i mchog 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // oM shang ka re shAn ti ka ro/ g+hu na g+hud Tak+Shur+tha ni g+hA ta ya g+hA ta ya/ g+hu Ti ni swA

56a4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad la legs so zhes bya ba byin nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom
56a5(rgyud): ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sngags kyi dngos grub thams cad dang / sku dang gsung dang thugs la mi gnas so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'on kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
56a6(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad sngags kyi dngos grub thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bdag gi lus dang ngag dang sems rdo rje la ni mi gnas so// lus dang ngag dang sems rdo
56a7(rgyud): rje de dag kyang / 'dod pa'i khams na mi gnas/ gzugs kyi khams na mi gnas/ gzugs med pa'i khams na mi gnas/ sems lus la mi gnas/ lus kyang sems la mi
56a8(rgyud): gnas/ ngag kyang sems la mi gnas/ sems kyang ngag la mi gnas so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nam mkha' ltar ngo bo nyid dag pa'i phyir ro// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
56b1(rgyud): kyis sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos gang la gnas/ gang nas byung / rang gi lus dang ngag dang sems las
56b2(rgyud): byung ngo // bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sems gang na gnas nam mkha' la gnas so// nam mkha' gang na gnas gang na yang mi gnas so// de nas sangs rgyas dang byang chub
56b3(rgyud): sems dpa' thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur rmad du gyur nas/ rang gi sems kyi chos nyid la gnas nas sems shing cang mi smra bar 'khod par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung
56b4(rgyud): dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las// / sems thams cad kyi dam tshig gi snying po'i rdo rje 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i le'u ste bcwo lnga pa'o// 
56b5(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus par gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa la/ 
56b6(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje dam tshig gis gsol ba btab nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje rin chen gyi mchod pa'i tshogs kyis mchod pa byas so// 
56b7(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ rdo rje thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor seng ge'i dam tshig gi rgyal po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rdo rje sku'i dkyil
56b8(rgyud): 'khor 'di sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lus phyung ngo // de nas sku'i dkyil 'khor mchog/ thugs kyi dkyil 'khor rab 'dra ba// dkyil 'khor rnams ni kun gyi
57a1(rgyud): / mchogalegs par rab tu bshad par bya// khru ni bcu drug tshad du bya// gru bzhi lham pa rab tu mdzes// sangs rgyas kun gyi dkyil 'khor te// sku yi rdo rje rab tu gnas// 
57a2(rgyud): de yi nang du 'khor lo ni// rdo rje'i tsho gas bri bar bya// sngags rnams kyis ni gsang ba mchog/ phyag na rdo rje'i gnas su bya// dbus su rnam par snang mdzad gnas// mi skyed pa la sogs pa'ang
57a3(rgyud): bri// sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje mchog/ gA rnams kun du dgod par bya// stobs can pha rol gnon pa yi// khro bo rnams kyang skar bri'o// rdo rje gsang ba rab bsgoms pas// mchod
57a4(rgyud): pa sngags shes pa yau bya// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// dam tshig shin du 'da' dka' ba'o// gshang dang gtse ba la sogs pa/ bye brag tu nges par dbul/ 'di ni sngag
57a5(rgyud): rnams thams cad kyi// sku yi rdo rje las dam tshig/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i dkyil 'khor ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa gsung rdo rje thos
57a6(rgyud): cad dam tshig gi sprin bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ gsung rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // de nas gsung gi dkyil
57a7(rgyud): 'a mam/ sngags kyi da/ sprul rab stsu //  'kho rnasas nabAn g+hu mtsho/ legs par ra tu bshud par gyu/ wAn shu nIng d+ha g+h+ra/ glu nam rkyog pan/ 
57b1(rgyud): dbang drug/ de dbus 'khor lo rgyun zin// zlum por kun du bri bar bya// mdo du phyag rgya thams cad ni// zlog bzhin du bri ba ga/ rgyu dbrag med pa'i phyag rgya che// de la dbus sgyu
57b2(rgyud): bzhag par bya// rdo rje'i gnas mchog de nyid du// thams cad yongs su dgod par bya// yongs su gsal ba cho ga bzhin// dkyil 'khor dam pa byas nas ni// de nas gsang ba
57b3(rgyud): mchod pa bya// 'on tang rdo rje can dag mnyes// gshang gni khu ba'i dam tshig gis// mchod na dngos grub thob par 'gyur// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// dam tshig shin du 'da'
57b4(rgyud): dka' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa kun nas sprin gyi tshogs rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
57b5(rgyud): la snyoms par zhugs nas/ rab tu gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor gsang ba 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsu dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // rdo rje mchog 'dzin gang yin pa'i// gzugs ni dbus su legs
57b6(rgyud): bris pa// de yi dkyil 'khor gnas su 'gyur// sku gsung thugs kyi gsang las byung // 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gnas ye shes gsang
57b7(rgyud): ba yin te rab tu gsang ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor thams cad 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sku dang
57b8(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gsong ba 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi sngags kyi snying po'i mdo'i yi ge'i tshig rnams so// oM AHt+ma/ 
58a1(rgyud): rdo rje'i thig ni gdab pa dang // tshon rtsi dag ni dge ba dang // sngags kyi sems dpas mi bya ste// byas na byang chub rnyed par bka'// de bas dam tshig tshul shes pas// sdug
58a2(rgyud): kyi lha rnams phab nas su// byin gyis brlabs kyis gnas bsgoms la// dkyil 'khor rnams ni rnam par brtag/ rgyal chen rnam par snang mdzad dang / yang na spyan ni dbab par bya/ 
58a3(rgyud): sku yi dkyil 'khor gnas yid 'ong // rdo rje'i sku yi yon tan 'thob// rdo rje chos ni rgyal po che// rang gi chos mas dbab par bya// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi gsang ba rab brtag pa
58a4(rgyud): yin/ rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// mA ma ki yang dbab par bya// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad kyi// gsang ba rmad du byung ba'o// de ltar byas na byin rlob cing // yid la dbang ba
58a5(rgyud): nyid gshegs te// rab tu dges par gyur nas ni// gsang ba dag gis mchog kyang gsol// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// sngags kyi sems dpas bya ba ni// rdo rje gsang ba rmad po che// 
58a6(rgyud): khro bo'i rgyal pos bkug nas ni// sangs rgyas thams cad mchod par bya// rdo rje dri med gsung dag gi/ dam tshig mchod pa dus gsum pa// rdo rje gsum gyi sbyor ba bya// sngags kyi dngos grub
58a7(rgyud): thob par byed// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// sngags rnams thams cad nyid la yang // rmad du byung ba'i gtor ma dbul// gshang gcisha dang 'bru mar dang // sems las byung ba'i tsan dang // 
58a8(rgyud): khu ba dag gis sngags rnams kun// tshim par 'gyur bar kun du bshad 'di ni dam tshig mchog yin te// sangs rgyas byang chub rdzogs byed pa'o// thig gdab pa yi cho ga 'di// bdag nyid
58b1(rgyud): gang tshe spyod pa ni// rnam par snang mdzad bsgoms nas su// rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu bsgom// yang na rdo rje mi 'chir grags// slob ma rdo rje 'od po che// sangs rgyas kun gyis nges bstan
58b2(rgyud): pa'i// las kyi go 'phang bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas rgyas rgyal chen lnga rnams ni// rdo rje'i thig skud dag la dgod// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba rab tu rmad byung ba'o//

58b7(rgyud): su rang gi lha yi gzugs// bsams te zhal du dbab par bya// 'di skad kyang gsungs so// dbang po gnyis kyi dam tshig gis// sbyin bsreg brgya rtsa brgyad du bya// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad
58b8(rgyud): kyidam tshig shin du 'da' dka' ba'o// rnam snang mdzad kyi sbyor ba yis// slob ma rdo rje gsum las byung // a ni lus dang ngag somos la// bsgoms nas rdo rjes gzung bar bya// rgyal chen rdorje
59a1(rgyud): sems dpa' dang grags chen rnam par snang mdzad dag/ sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig du// byin gyis brlabs ni rab tu gsol// de la 'di ni dkyil 'khom
59a2(rgyud): chen por 'jug pa'i rdo rje'i tshig go// a khaM bI ra hUM/ 'di ni dam tshig thams cad kyi lus dang ngag dang sems rdo rje'i snying po'o// de la 'di ni rdo rje chen po dbang bskur ba'i gsang

59a4(rgyud): gsungs so// rdo rje skra gsum sngags kyis ni// yungs kar dag gis gdab par bya// de la de ya chen ni// bdag nyid dbang bskur rab tu stsol// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyis//

59a8(rgyud): ga gsang ba'o// byang chub rdo rje sangs rgyas la// mchod chen ji ltar stsal ba bzhin// bdag kyang rab tu bsgrol ba'i phyir// nam mkha'i rdo rje dang bdage stsol// de tshe de la dbang bskur/

59b4(rgyud): tshig mchog tu rtag pa'o// sngags kyi skul ba smras ma yis// de la sngags kyang sbyin par bya// sngags kyi rgyal po'i ting 'dzin dang // gsang ba sbyin pa brtsam par bya// khu ba 'am yang na gshang ba'ang

59b6(rgyud): gzugs// sems can don spyod phyir gnas pa'o// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sngags mnyes par bya ba gsang ba'o// glang po'i sha dang rta yi / sha chen dag kyang bza' bya zhing //

59b8(rgyud): dge gis// sngogs nam sa kun gyi yi ge mo// bsgoms na de ma thog tu ya // bcom ldan 'das sngags kyi rog pa'i skyes bu chen pas de skad ba/ 'a stsal to// dngas grub thams cad bsgrub pa da
60a1(rgyud): dam tshig chen po bsgrub pa dang // sangs rgyas byang chub nyid dag kyang // nan tan du ni bsgrub par bya// mi snang stebs dang brtson 'grus dang // rdo rje 'gugs pa mchog dag kyang

60a4(rgyud): po'o// nam mkha' rdo rje dbus su bsam// sangs rgyas kun gyis nam mkha'i khams// yongs su gang bar rnam par sgom// de yi sku gsung thugs kyi gnas// der ni sngags kyis dbab par

61b1(rgyud): thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // tsuM/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ni// nam mkha'i rdo rje dbus su bsam// sangs rgyas sprin gyi cho gu yis// rdo rje gsum gyi grags chen ni// lus dang ngag dang sems la
61b2(rgyud): dbab/ bskul byed rdo rje ma bsgom mo// rgyan rnams thams cad yongs rdzogs pa// kha dog dkar mo rab tu sgom// rdo rje sems dpa' rgyal po che// bsams la sngags kyi tshig dgod do// rdo rje'i

61b6(rgyud): sangs rgyas lnga yi cho ga yis// gnas lnga dag du bsgom par bya// rdo rje bdud rtsi chu de yi// bsam gtan gnas la 'dug la dbul// rdo rje sems dpa'i cho ga yis// dbu brgyan de la rnam par
61b7(rgyud): bsam// de ltar byas na gnod sbyin dbang // gnod gnas dbang po 'od che ni mnyes// rdo rje dam tshig gi phyag rgya rdzas bsgrub pa'i tog gi dpal zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// de nas bcom ldan 'das
61b8(rgyud): phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje'i 'dod pa nye bar spyod pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i tirjeng 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ gnod sbyin mo'i dam tshig gi tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs
62a1(rgyud): @rdo rje las phyung ngo // k+ShiM mkha' dbyings rdo rje dbus gnas par// glu bzhi lham par rab tu bzang // thams cad rin chen bzhi las byas// me tog spos kyis kun du 'khrigs// gnod sbyin
62a2(rgyud): mo ni thams cad kyis// na mkha'i dbyings ni gang bar bsam// gzugs kyi sprin dag rnam bsams la// rdo rje gsum gyi sbyor bas dbab// las gsum rdo rje'i bye brag gis// de yi bsam gtan bsgom
62a3(rgyud): par bya/ rdo rje 'jam pa'i ting 'dzin gnas// dbu rgyun la ni khro bo bsam// snying khar sngags kyi tshig bsgoms la// rdo rje'i sbyor ba brtsam par bya// gnod sbyin mo thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid du
62a4(rgyud): gnas pa'i bsgom pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje'i sngags thams cad kyi dngos grub kyi rnam par 'phrul ba'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i
62a5(rgyud): ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dngos grub phra mo 'di nyid kyi// sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku dang gsung dang thugs yang dag 'grub// sangs rgyas gzugs 'dzin 'od bzang
62a6(rgyud): po// 'dzam bu chu bo gser 'od 'dra// dngos grub phra mo dag la gnas// mi snang bas ni yang dag 'grub// 'jam pa'i 'od dang 'dra bar 'gyur// gnod sbyin rgyal po grub pa che// rig 'dzin
62a7(rgyud): dag gi dbang por 'gyur// de la 'di ni rdo rje dngos grub thams cad kyi gzugs gsang ba'i dngos grub rnams so// sngags kyi dngos grub thob pa yi// mdzes pa'i gzugs rnams thams cad ni/ 
62a8(rgyud): 'jig rten khams ni thams cad du// mthong ba nyid kyis dga' bar 'gyur// tsug tor thams cad 'grub pa ni// yid bzhin nor bu'i bdag por 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub byed pa'i mchog
62b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas rdo rje rab sgom pa'o// bcom ldan 'das bsam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa shin gshes pam sa kyis
62b2(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsugs kyi rig pa'i brtul zhugs yang dag par len pa'i spyod pa 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang bu rdo las phyung ngo // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje las// lus dang
62b3(rgyud): ngag sems sgom pa ni// rang tshul nyid kyis de bya ste// de ltar dngos grub 'thob par 'gyur// de la 'di ni sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i rig pa'i brtul zhugs so// thor btsugs dbu rgyan can
62b4(rgyud): gyi gzugs// chen po khu dog dkar po 'dra// sngags kyi sdom pas kun du bsdams// cho ga bzhin du thams cad bya// lo grangs bcu drug lon pa ni// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par klubs// bzhin
62b5(rgyud): stug mig gi grus ring ba// rnyed nas rig pa'i brtul zhugs skyed// spyan gyi go 'phang longs spyod cing // rdo rje'i mtshan mas bsgom par bya// phyag rgya sngags kyi cho ga shes// sngags kyi rgyud ni legs
62b6(rgyud): par bslabs// de bzhin gshegs pa'i btsun mor bya// sangs rgyas byang chub la rab gnas// brtul zhugs chen pos dus bzhir ni// gsang ba'i mchod pa rab tu bya// sdong bu rtsa ba 'bras bu yi// 
62b7(rgyud): bza' dang bca' ba spyad par bya// 'on tang myur du sangs rgyas 'gyur// bdag po ye shes rgya mtsho che// zla ba drug gi de dag kun// gdon mi za bar 'thob par 'gyur// rtag tu gzhan gyi nor rku zhing // gsad
62b8(rgyud): gsad pa'ang rmad du byung ba dang // 'dod chags rdo rje'i gnas spyod pa// sdom pa 'di ni kun du bsdams// 'dod chags rdo rje lcags kyu mo// yon tan lug rgyud mA ma ki/ gsung gi rdo rje thugs mchog
63a1(rgyud): la/ 'di ni rnam pa kun du rigs// bsam gtan yig gsum rdo rje can// rang gi phyag rgya 'am sems kyis bsam// de ltar sangs rgyas kun mkhyen pa// mnyes par 'gyur/ 
63a2(rgyud): bar gdon mi za// bsgrub pa po ni blo brtan pas// nags tshal dag tu bsod snyoms blang // kha zas bzang po ster ba dag/ de dag skrag nas ster bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i bdag nyid gsum 'das na
63a3(rgyud): rdo rje yi ge 'jig par 'gyur// lha mo klu mo gnod sbyin mo lha ma yin namaM mi mo 'ang rung // rnyed nas rig pa'i brtul zhugs bya// rdo rje gsum gyis ye shes sten// 'di ni sngags rnams thams cad
63a4(rgyud): kyi/ de nyid gsang ba'i tshul chen yin// rdo rje gsum gyi ye shes 'byung // sangs rgyas byang chub rab 'jug pa// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rig pa'i brtul zhugs kyi
63a5(rgyud): dam tshig de kho na nyid kyi rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rab tu gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las// // dngos grub
63a6(rgyud): thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor rdo rje mngon par byang chub pa zhes bya ba'i le'u ste bcu drug pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang 'dus nas/ 
63a7(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba btab pa// mi bskyod rdo rje ye shes che// rdo rje dbyings ni mkhas pa che// rdo rje
63a8(rgyud): gsum mchog dkyil 'khor gsum// rdo rje'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal li// rnam par snang mdzad dag pa che// rdo rje zhi ba dga' ba che// rang bzhin 'od gsal mchog gi mchog/ ston pa rdo rje
63b1(rgyud): phyag 'tshal lo// rin chen rgyal po rab tu zab// rdo rje nam mkha' dri ma med// rang bzhin dag pa gos pa med// rdo rje'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje dpag med rgyal po che// mi rtog nam mkha' rdo rje 'dzin
63b2(rgyud): 'dod chags pha rol phyin pa brnyes// rdo rje gsung la phyag 'tshal lo// don yod rdo rje rdzogs sangs rgyas// bsam pa thams cad rdzogs mdzad pa// dag pa ngo bo nyid las byung // rdo rje sems dpa' phyag
63b3(rgyud): 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas kun gyis bskul ba yi// stod tshig zhi ba 'di rnams kyis// rdo rje'i longs spyod stod na ni// de'ang sangs rgyas 'dra bar 'gyur// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// sangs rgyas kun
63b4(rgyud): la rjes brtse ba// rdo rje gsang ba gsung dag pa// rdo rje'i gsung ni bka' stsal pa// e ma ho sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// chos kyi dbyings ni yi ge che// rang bzhin 'od gsal yongs su dag/ naM mkha'i
63b5(rgyud): dbyings bzhin dri ma med// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lhas phyung ngo // sangs
63b6(rgyud): rgyas ye shes rgya mtsho yis// dam tshig bzhi ni bsrung bar bya// sha chen brtag tu bza' bar bya// 'di ni dam tshig mchog yin no// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag pos/ sangs rgyas thos
63b7(rgyud): cad kyi gsung gi rdo rje'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dam tshig bzhi po bsrung bar bya// gsung gi rdo rje yi ge che// gshang gci dag ni rtag tu bza'// 'di ni gsang
63b8(rgyud): barmad byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos rdo rje 'dzin thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // rdo rje sems dpa' rdzu
64a1(rgyud): 'phrul ches dam tshig bzhi po srung bar bya// khrag dang khru sgyur ba dag/ brtul zhugs brtan pas brtag tu bza'// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yos// dam tshig 'di ni rmang pon
64a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi rtag pa 'di// rdo rje 'dzin gyis bsrung bar bya// gang zhig dam tshig 'di bsrung ba// rdo rje sems dpa' 'od po che// de yi sku gsung thugs rtogs pa// de ma thag tu sangs rgyas 'gyur// 
64a3(rgyud): de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rang sangs rgyas kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // de yi lus kyi ston pa ni// rdo rje'i sku la rab tu
64a4(rgyud): gnas/ sems can bzud pa'i ngang tshul te// dam tshig mchog tu brtag pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos nyan thos kyi bslab pa'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang
64a5(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam// byed pa ye shes spangs pa rnams// dman par mos pa thams cad kyi// dam tshig 'di ni rmad po che// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs
64a6(rgyud): ma thams cad kyi bdag pos/ tshangs pa'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // gti mug lam gyi las gang rnams// byed pa 'jigs shing mi sdug pa// sangs rgyas byang
64a7(rgyud): chub ston pa ste// sku yi rdo rje nyid du 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ drag po'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // khams gsum
64a8(rgyud): dag na gnas pa yi// bud med rdo rje las byung rnams// sna tshogs dngos pos sprad pa ni// dam tshig mchog tu rmad byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ khyab
64b1(rgyud): 'jug gi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // sems can las byung ji snyed pa// dbyer med sku gsum la gnas pa// rdo rje'i mkha' dbyings bdag nyid kyang // bsam gtan rdo rjes bas
64b2(rgyud): par bya/ de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rang gi dam tshig gi rdo rje 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku yi rdo rje tshangs par 'gyur// gsung gi rdo rje
64b3(rgyud): dbang phyug che// thugs kyi rgyal po rdo rje 'dzin// de nyid khyab 'jug rdzu 'phrul che// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ gnod sbyin mo thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi
64b4(rgyud): sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // khrag dang sha ni za ba dang // rtag tu gzhan gyi bud med spyod// dam tshig dka' ba 'di rnams kyis// rdo rje chen po mnyes par bya// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin
64b5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ klu'i rgyal po rnams kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // 'o ma 'thung ba phra ma can// de dag 'dod dang dril 'bad// dam tshig 'dis
64b6(rgyud): ni bsgrub par bya// gzhan du nges par nyon mongs 'gyur// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ lha ma yin gyi bu mo'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje
64b7(rgyud): las phyung ngo // khro zhing nga rgyal gsod pas gnon// spos dang me tog spyod las skyes// rdo rjes 'og dam tshig ste// gdul dka' rdo rje 'jigs pa po// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams
64b8(rgyud): cad kyi bdag pos/ srin mo rnams kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // thod rus bdug pa'i 'bru mar dang // zhag gis rab tu dga' bar 'gyur// 'byung po kun gyi dam
65a1(rgyud): tshig ste/ dag byed 'di ni don chen byed// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang
65a2(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // gshang gci dang ni khrag dag bza'// chang la sogs pa'ang rtag tu btung // rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyor ba yis// gnas kyi mtshan nyid gyis bsad bya// ngo bo
65a3(rgyud): nyid kyis kun 'byung ba// khams gsum dag na rnam par spyod// sems can kun la phan 'dod pa'o// dam tshig ma lus spyad par bya// khams gsum pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig gi rjes
65a4(rgyud): su 'brang ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos lus kyi dngos grub kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // 
65a5(rgyud): lus kyi rnam gsum thams cad ni// rdo rje las ni byung bar bya// sems can khams ni thams cad du// rtag par sangs rgyas sku byed pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams
65a6(rgyud): cad kyi bdag pos/ ngag gi dngos grub kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // tshig gi las lam ma lus par// khams gsum dri med dkyil 'khor te// tshig gi
65a7(rgyud): dngos grub yid 'ong 'di// dam tshig shin du 'da' dka' ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sems rdo rje'i dam tshig dngos grub 'di nyid kyi sku dang
65a8(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // yid kyi rdo rje'i rang bzhin kun// rdo rje brtan pa 'dzin pas bsgoms// rdo rje mi phyed gsum ldan gyis// dam tshig bshad pa 'di yin no// bcom ldan 'das
65b1(rgyud): kun du mdzes dga' rdo rje sems dpas de skad bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sngags thams cad kyi rdo rje'i snying po'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang / 
65b2(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // rang rgyal nyan thos de bzhin te// sku gsung thugs su sbyor ba na// phyag 'tshal na ni ma rung 'gyur// de nas yang
65b3(rgyud): phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bsam gtan gyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // kun du rdo rje sems dpa' yi// sku gsung
65b4(rgyud): thugs kyi dkyil 'khor la// bsam gtan rdo rje gsum sbyor bas// sngags zlos pas ni bsam gtan bya// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sngags bsgrub mo'i
65b5(rgyud): dam tshig dang sdom pa nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // mdor na sems can khams rnams ni// bsam gtan rdo rjes bskul bar bya// rdo rje gsum gyi phyag 'tshal mchog/ dam
65b6(rgyud): tshig rdo rje las byung ba'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ bsnyen pa dang / bsgrub pa dang / nye bar bsgrub pa dang / bsgrub pa chen po'i sdom pa nyid kyi sku dang gsung
65b7(rgyud): dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // rdo rje gshang gcis nam mkha'i dbyings// yongs su gang bar rnam par bsam// dus gsum rdo rje dag la dbul// dam tshig rab tu rtag pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo
65b8(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rdo rje mi snang ba thams cad kyi mi snang ba'i dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // dus bzhir ji ltar mchog bzhin du// rdo rje mo
66a1(rgyud): ni nyin re spyad// yang na rdzas kyang rtag tu dbrog/ dam tshig rdo rje rdzogs byed pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ nam mkha'i rigs
66a2(rgyud): 'dzin gyi tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje ni// dbu brgyan dag la bsam gtan bsam// rdo rje gsum gyi dam tshig ste// khros pa rnams kyis mi
66a3(rgyud): thub po/ de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ sngags 'chang las dang po pa thams cad kyi dam tshig 'di nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // sku yi rdo
66a4(rgyud): rje'i kha zas la// phyi rol rdo rje 'dzin pa dang // mdo gdon cho ga bya ba la// rtag par rdo rje chos su bya// bcom ldan 'das ngo bo nyid dag pa rdo rjes de skad bka' stsal to// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin
66a5(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos/ rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi snying po rdo rje mnyam pa nyid rnam par dgongs nas/ cang mi gsung bar gyur to// de nas yang brjod du
66a6(rgyud): med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ri rab kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad
66a7(rgyud): ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'di ci'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi nang na cang mi gsung bar
66a8(rgyud): bzhugs/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gsheg pa cad kyi sku dang gsung dang
66b1(rgyud): thugs kyi bdag po 'di sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ngo bo nyid dmigs su med pa'i yi ge'i tshig la// ngo bo nyid med pa'i yi ge'i tshig brjod nas mi gsung bar bzhugs so// rigs kyi bu de bzhin
66b2(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'di sems pa na 'di snyam du gyur to// sku mi 'gyur ba ma skyes pa/ gsung dang thugs kyang mtshan ma med// nam mkha'i rdo rjer rtog las byung // log par gzung
66b3(rgyud): pas zin pa yin// de nas 'jam dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa de dag la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin
66b4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad gsung rdo rje'i tshig la/ phyin ci log kun 'byung ba mi brtag tu gsol// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams
66b5(rgyud): cad kyi rdo rje dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid spyod par 'gyur ba'i rjes su 'gro ba'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ tshangs pa la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mngon par shes pa chen po'i ye shes
66b6(rgyud): 'thob pa rnams chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid kyi ngo bo nyid mi shes nas/ 'di snyam du rnam par rtog to// ci rdo rje'i bdag nyid 'di de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos rdo rje de kho na nyid yongs su ma
66b7(rgyud): shes nas/ gsang ba'i yi ge rnams 'chad dam snyam du sems pa yang ma mchis so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces
66b8(rgyud): ces bka' stsal to// byang chub sems dpa' khyed rnams lta ci smos te/ nged de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i gsang ba mi 'gyur ba rnyed pa'ang sku dang gsung thugs kyi
67a1(rgyud): byang chub mi shes so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ skye ba med pa'i rdo rje mngon par byang chub pa ni ngo bo nyid med pa mi 'gyur ba las byung ba'o// rigs kyi bu sems can chen po'i khong
67a2(rgyud): su gtog pI sems can ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad byang chub la gnas pa sangs rgyas rdo rje'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye ma'o sems can de dag ni sku gsum rdo rje'i chos nyid kyi phyir sku dang
67a3(rgyud): gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ye shes thob pa'o// de nas phyag ni rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i ye shes thob pa'o// de nas phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa
67a4(rgyud): thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang // byang chub sems dpa' de de dag la 'di skad gsungs so// rang bzhin dag pa bdag mod

90a3(rgyud): kyis sad par byed// sku gsung thugs rje gcig/ de rnams skye bar bzhed pa yis// byang chub sems kyi ngo bo yis// rdo rje'i sngags su mdzad par gyur// rig pa'i skyes bu'i gzugs
90a4(rgyud): dag ni/ sngags kyis byin brlabs bla ma med// der ni zhal gsum pa lta bur// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gzigs// de nas mgon po bcom ldan gyi// thugs rjes bzhugs pa las byung
90a5(rgyud): ste/ byang chub sems ni rab bskor ba// lan gsum ched du brjod par mdzad// bsam mi khyab cing gnas med gang // de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // rdo rje byang chub sems gcig/ 
90a6(rgyud): las// spyod yul der ni gyur pa yin// de nas gsang tshul thos pa dang // de 'og gsang ba'i bdag pos ni// khyab bdag rnam par snang mdzad la// ji bzhin tshul du de btud zhus// phung

90b1(rgyud): zhig phyi dus skye bo yis// 'di dag 'tshal bar mi 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan rdo rje can// 'od chen ldan pas bka' stsal pa// ma 'ongs skye bo mthong nas ni// gang zhig khyod kyis nga dris pa// 
90b2(rgyud): legs so legs so legs pa che// gsang ba'i bdag po khyed legs so// smras don ji lta ji lta bar// de ltar khyod la lung bstan bya// mi 'ongs dus su ma rnams ni// 'jig rten rgyang phan
90b3(rgyud): mchog gzhol 'gyur// log par lta ba la gnas te// tso dga' bar yang spyod par byed// la la glu dang gar la dga'// rgod dang bsreg la mchog tu gzhol// dri dang phreng ba la dga' zhing //

90b5(rgyud): dag 'dod par 'gyur// nya dang sha dang de bzhin chang // gshang gci khu khrag rnams ni// skyes bu glen pa za byed cing // med par smra ba chos su sgrogs// ma dang sring mo la sogs pa/ 
90b6(rgyud): bgrod min la ni bgrod pa dang // pha dang ma yang gsod pa dang // de bzhin srog chags gzhan rnams gsod// brdzun gyi tshig nyid smra ba dang // khyad par du yang rku ba dang // gzhan gyi chung ma'i/ 
90b7(rgyud): thad 'gro zhing // smad pa gzhan yang byed par 'gyur// la la dam chos spong ba dang // de bzhin mtshams med byed pa ste// sna tshogs sdig pa byas nas kyang // sngags pa dngos grub

91a1(rgyud): de/ mi bzad sdig pa byas pa dang // log par lta la mchog gzhol rnams// ngan song gsum du 'gro bar 'gyur// de rnams rjes su gzung ba'i phyir// gsang ba 'di ltar
91a2(rgyud): bstan pa yin// gang zhig yang dag thob pa nyid// 'dir ni de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur// gsang ba'i bdag po mkhas rnams kyis// tshul mchog 'drenani rnyed gyur nas// don gsal yang
91a3(rgyud): dag rnyed pa dang // de yang nga rgyal dag tu ltung // de rnams ting 'dzin zhi nyid dang // shes rab nyid kyang shin du ring // rab tu dga' dang ldan pa yis// rnal 'byor pa bdag yin zhes smra//

91b5(rgyud): ni ston par byed// de rnams yang dag sdud byed pa'i// gsang ba'i dgongs pas bshad pa yin// dam tshig nyams te gnas pa rnams// 'di yis thams cad dgug par bya// rang gi rjes
91b6(rgyud): rig mi shes na// de rnams zhi bar ga la 'gyur// de bas rjes su gzung don du// tshul 'di dag ni gyur pa yin// de nas bcom ldan de bzhin gshogs// gcig tu 'dus par gyur nas su// 
91b7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs kun bdag po la// rang mchod de nyid dam tshig sbyin// yang dag byung bas legs mchod de// phyag 'tshal nas ni 'di skad gsol// de bzhin gshegs pa gsang ba mchog
